藍嘉寳的心境（二） 260

— 希雋

儘在黑袍子背　後邊悄悄地說着說着說着。抽着烟，聽笛子吹起了一雙急促的Ｔａｎｇｏ，流覽跟前一幅明媚的肉色風物景。性感覺受了劇烈的刺激，越來越有按捺不住的樣兒。爲要抵抗這種不良症的暴發，有時就下意識地闔了眼珠子。祇讓聽覺感官陶醉在一支迂緩而婉媚的Ｗａｌｔｓ中，而卡爾已經到了非跳不可的時候，他簡直𤍠中了的，他說：

丨丨喂，都來一雙吧。

丨丨又中了不良症了。

丨丨到這兒乾坐着就不如不來呵！

燈光打的滅了，卡爾巴的先開記錄。

卡爾平時是誇張他性昇華的，一面精緻光滑的肉體擺在眼前，他能够呌性細胞不開花，而此刻他却又做了一次被征服的俘虜，感官享樂的魁力呵！

是啦，躺在生活的激流上掙扎而感到疲乏的人們，都嗜愛借着此含蓄的形式求得性食慾的排洩，如像咱們一同地。每夜每夜差不多都浸在這些地方，這些色彩馥郁的地方。然而當那音樂没了，歌聲没了，肩挨肩没勁兒彳亍於回家的岑寂的夜行道上，聽夜風咻咻地吹打着西洋梧桐的葉子，葉子一片一片墮落地上，遠遠地，近近地，就你送着靑春落日的蛩鈴緩緩地飄去，飄去，這時候灌在心頭上的寂寞味只有自家兒知道呵！

1934.07.09

Opening of Through Train Service Between Peiping and Mukden: Japanese Guards Withdrawing from Train; Trial Period Ends Yesterday; After Negotiations Between Yin Tong and Japanese Side, We Are Fully Responsible for the Section Within the Pass 1

(Peiping) Regarding the issue of Japanese guards accompanying the Peiping-Mukden through train, the agreed trial period ended yesterday. Yin Tong negotiated with Staff Officer Kikuchi of the Japanese Garrison Headquarters in Tientsin. Simultaneously, due to the arrival of Japanese Commander Umezu in Peiping, the Political Readjustment Committee specially dispatched Liu Shi-sun to negotiate with him. Umezu agreed to withdraw the guards as scheduled, and yesterday notified the Japanese Garrison. Today, the Peiping-Mukden through train departing from Peiping will not have Japanese guards. The Peiping-Mukden train arriving in Peiping today departed from Mukden the day before yesterday. The Japanese guards on the train disembarked at Tanggu upon receiving orders from the Japanese military authorities. (Eighth Dispatch)

(Tientsin) Starting today, the withdrawal of Japanese guards from the Peiping-Mukden through train will be implemented. The safety of passengers on the section within the Pass will be the full responsibility of the Peiping-Mukden Railway Bureau. The bureau has today ordered all railway police along the line to strictly inspect passengers boarding the through train after they purchase their tickets before allowing them to pass. A supervisor and ten policemen are assigned to each train to observe passengers with suspicious behavior and conduct inspections at any time. This afternoon at 4:00 PM, Yin Tong visited Japanese Commander Umezu stationed in Tientsin to discuss the safety of passengers on the through train, exchanging many opinions. Yin originally intended to take the train to Peiping tonight to meet with Shibayama, but was unable to do so due to circumstances. He plans to go on the 10th. (Eighth Dispatch)

(Peiping) After Yin Tong negotiated with Shibayama yesterday, the Japanese guards on the Peiping-Mukden train have been withdrawn from the 8th. We are fully responsible for the section within the Pass. (Eighth Dispatch from Central News Agency)

(Tientsin) The Oriental Travel Agency established in Shanhaikuan was finally organized by the 8th. It is divided into four departments, each with two Chinese and Japanese section chiefs. There are thirty-seven staff members, sixteen Chinese and twenty-one Japanese. Most of the Japanese staff are transferred from the South Manchuria Railway and the International Tourist Bureau. Each time the through train passes through Shanhaikuan, the travel agency sends personnel to the station to assist. There is also an information desk set up inside the station to provide passengers with information. (Eighth Dispatch)

(Peiping) Regarding the withdrawal of Japanese guards from the Peiping-Mukden through train, which is due today, the original agreement was for a one-week period. Whether they will withdraw as agreed tomorrow, according to the Japanese side, the original agreement for Japanese guards accompanying the train was for one week. If no accidents occur during this period, they will be abolished immediately. However, because incidents endangering trains have occurred frequently between Tanggu and Tangshan, there are currently no preparations for withdrawal. This morning, the Japanese guards on the Peiping-Mukden trains departing from and arriving in Peiping carried three light machine guns. It is reported that Yin Tong contacted Japanese military official Shibayama by long-distance telephone from Tientsin this afternoon to negotiate. (Full Day Dispatch)

(Peiping) The Oriental Travel Agency in Shanhaikuan has been doing good business recently. The agency's address has now been renovated. In addition to the Japanese Deputy Manager Hirayama, there are also several Japanese employees, including Kojima. These Japanese all reside at the Donghai Hotel in Shanhaikuan. The signboard of the Oriental Travel Agency was written by Yuan Tai, the magistrate of Linyu County. (Seventh Dispatch)

(Peiping) According to postal officials, since the opening of the Peiping-Mukden through train, the number of letters transmitted by China Post through Shanhaikuan to the South Manchuria Railway area outside the Pass has increased by a quarter, averaging more than 35,000 pieces per day. More than 20,000 pieces are also imported into the interior. They are transported from the Peiping-Mukden train to Tientsin and Peiping, where they are received by the Chinese Post Office. Most of the stamps affixed to the letters are Japanese stamps. Many postal items are also unloaded at Shanhaikuan. The losses currently incurred by China amount to several hundred thousand yuan per month. Transmitting mail to Europe and America via sea routes or via Vladivostok through Siberia is very slow. If postal services are to be resumed, the first step is to restore international postal schedules and handle postal money orders between the Northeast and the interior. Due to the complexity of the procedures, this will not be done for the time being. Regarding the establishment of tax checkpoints at the Great Wall, the Ministry of Finance has ordered the Tientsin Customs to handle it. Chilton, the British tax commissioner of Qinhuangdao, is currently in contact with Igi, the chief of the Kwantung Army Shanhaikuan Special Affairs Agency. It is expected that it will be established at the beginning of next month. Zhang Yongnian, the deputy tax commissioner dispatched by the Ministry of Finance for inspection, is currently investigating in Qinhuangdao and Shanhaikuan. (Seventh Dispatch)

National Mining, Metallurgy, and Geology Exhibition Opens Yesterday; More Than 50,000 Items on Display; Thirty-One Pavilions Open Simultaneously; Chen Gongbo Arrives in Tientsin to Attend Opening Ceremony 2

(Tientsin) The Mining, Metallurgy, and Geology Exhibition opened at 9:00 AM this morning. Chairman Chen Gongbo, along with more than 600 people from all walks of life and representatives from academic institutions, attended. After Chen finished his report, Wang Zhengting delivered a speech on behalf of the Central Government, urging the people to cooperate in mining. Yu Xuezhong, representing the Hebei Education Department, and Zhou Binglin, representing others, also gave speeches. The meeting adjourned at 12:00 PM. Telegrams of congratulations from Wang Jingwei, Chiang Kai-shek, and various ministers were received today and read aloud by Li Shutian, the chief executive of the exhibition. Afterwards, photographs were taken and the exhibition was visited for a week before dispersing. A total of more than 50,000 items are on display at the Mining Exhibition. Products from famous mines in the country have been collected, and foreign countries such as Germany, Sweden, Britain, and the United States have also sent products for display. They are divided into thirty-one pavilions. It has been open to the public since 2:00 PM this afternoon. (Eighth Dispatch)

(Tientsin) Chen Gongbo reported at the Mining Exhibition, stating: 1. China's coal reserves are 248 million tons, ranking third in the world. Coal mines with permits for mining total 11 million hectares, while other non-metallic mining areas total 1.8 million hectares. Therefore, coal mines account for 86% of the mining area. Before the September 18th Incident, the annual output was more than 20 million tons. Last year, due to the loss of 7 million tons of output in the Northeast, it was slightly worse. The domestic consumption is 20 million tons per year, so imports exceeded 1.3 million tons last year. 2. China's steel industry ranks ninth in the world, with a domestic annual output of 2,300 tons, necessitating the supplementation of foreign steel. The annual value of imports exceeds 70-80 million yuan. Today, people from the industrial and financial sectors are here, hoping to make efforts to assist the industrial sector to develop. (Eighth Dispatch)

(Tientsin) Chen Gongbo arrived in Tientsin at 4:20 AM this morning and is staying at the Empress Hotel. He is here only to attend the opening ceremony of the Mining Exhibition and has no other business. He is scheduled to return to Nanjing by train on the evening of the 9th. This morning, Wang Zhengting arrived in Tientsin on behalf of the Central Party Department to attend the Mining Exhibition. Chen Gongbo said that the Ministry of Industry's ten-year national industrial plan is being drafted and cannot be announced until it becomes a reality. However, China is different from the Soviet Union, and the implementation of the plan cannot be forcibly imitated. Regarding the construction of a steel plant, the procedures have some minor problems and are being discussed with the British. It will be realized soon. This afternoon at 4:00 PM, Chen broadcast news about the Mining Exhibition. To facilitate visitors, the Mining Exhibition has agreed with the Peiping-Mukden Railway and the municipal government to add special train and bus services to Xigu every day, with very low fares, until the closing day. (Eighth Dispatch)

Chiang Expected to Arrive in Jiujiang Last Night 3

(Nanjing) Chairman Chiang Kai-shek took the Yingrui warship from Nanjing to Jiujiang on the evening of the 7th. He passed Wuhu that night and met the Xianning warship, which departed from Nanjing at 5:00 PM on the 7th. The Xianning followed behind to escort him. They proceeded from Wuhu to Jiujiang and are expected to arrive in Jiujiang on the evening of the 8th. After arriving, Chiang will go to Lotus Cave and then to Guling. (Eighth Dispatch from Central News Agency)

Judicial Yuan Interprets Legal Provisions 4

(Nanjing) The Judicial Yuan has unified the interpretation of laws and regulations regarding the authority of the head of the household over property and various doubts about establishing an heir. (1) The head of the household manages household affairs and, for the benefit of the entire family, may dispose of family property. However, property that has already been inherited by family members or that belongs to them requires the consent of the family members. (2) Before the implementation of the inheritance section of the Civil Code, a widow who remained chaste could establish an heir for her husband. According to the laws at the time, she should obtain the consent of the direct ascendants of her husband. If consent was not sought in advance, her ascendants could request revocation. However, they could still supplement by seeking consent later. If they disagree without legitimate reasons, a judgment may be used to replace it. (Eighth Dispatch)

Tao Shangming Visits Shibayama to Continue Discussions on War Zone Issues; Replacement of the New Peace Preservation Corps to be Discussed After Huang Returns North; Japanese Side Decides to Ban Activities of Japanese and Korean Rōnin in Various Counties; Japanese Side Gives No Definite Indication Regarding the Transfer of Malanyu; Decision to Expand the Organization of the Committee for the Preservation of Eastern Tombs 5

(Peiping) Regarding the unresolved issues of the war zone, Tao Shangming came to Peiping after the implementation of the Peiping-Mukden through train to repeatedly meet with Yin Rugeng for negotiations and to negotiate with the Japanese side. However, there have been no concrete results. Tao visited Shibayama today to continue discussing these issues. 1. Regarding the replacement of the New Peace Preservation Corps, the Japanese side stated that the situation is complicated and not easy to resolve in a short time. It needs to be discussed further after Huang returns north. 2. Regarding the activities of Japanese and Korean Rōnin in various counties, Tanaka, the deputy consul of Japan in Tianjin, had previously gone to investigate with Kang Xuan, a consultant to the Jiji Mi Special Commissioner's Office, and had already taken measures to ban them. Recently, the Japanese consul notified our side that in the future, whether Japanese or Koreans come to the war zone to do business or travel, they must obtain a certificate from the Japanese consulate in Tianjin before they can enter. The Chinese side can protect them according to the law. If Japanese or Koreans enter the war zone without a consular certificate, the Chinese side can deport them. 3. Regarding the Malanyu issue, because the Japanese side has not yet given a definite indication of the transfer, the handover date has not yet been decided. Due to the recent heavy rains, the roads are difficult to travel, and Yin Tixin has postponed his trip. He will proceed as soon as he receives a definite reply from the Japanese side. 4. Regarding the preservation of the Eastern Tombs, it has been decided to expand the organization of the Preservation Committee, designating Wei Jian, Director of the Department of Civil Affairs of Hebei Province, Lin Chengxiu, Director of the Department of Industry, Yin Rugeng, Jiji Mi Special Commissioner, Li Chao, Magistrate of Xinglong County, Yin Tixin, Director of the Malanyu Office, and six representatives of the deposed Qing imperial family as ex officio members, with Yin Rugeng serving as chairman. Bao Ming was originally a representative of the Qing imperial family, but due to his old age, it has been decided to select someone else to participate, with Zaitao being the most promising candidate. Our side is responsible for the preservation rights and repair of the Eastern Tombs to restore the historical sites, but the deposed Qing imperial family can freely pay tribute to the Eastern Tombs. (Eighth)

(Peiping) At the Sino-Japanese representatives' meeting in Shanhaikuan, it was agreed that the unresolved issues in the war zone would be gradually discussed and resolved after the Peiping-Mukden through train was opened. Now that the through train has been implemented, Tao Shangming and Yin Rugeng have repeatedly met to discuss the steps for negotiations in the war zone and telegraphed Huang for instructions, preparing to conduct overall negotiations with the Japanese side. However, the Tanggu Truce Agreement is a kind of temporary military condition mutually respected. After all the post-war matters are resolved, it will lose its effect. Up to this year, we have completed everything that we should have fulfilled, but the Japanese army is entrenched inside the Great Wall line and has not complied with the agreement to withdraw from nine places: Jiumenkou, Luanxian, Lengkou, Taitouying, Jianchangying, Cuoheqiao, Xifengkou, Malanyu, and Gubeikou. Each place has 40-50 to 300-400 Japanese troops stationed there. The issue of the existence and abolition of the truce agreement is of great importance. All unresolved issues can only be concretely advanced after Huang returns north. (Eighth Dispatch)

(Peiping) It has been decided that Malanyu will be handed over on the 18th. Yin Rugeng met with Tao Shangming today to discuss matters. He will go to Malanyu on the 15th to participate in the handover ceremony. The issue of expanding the Malanyu Preservation Committee is currently being discussed by the provincial government, the Jiji Mi Commissioner's Office, the Xinglong County Government, and the deposed Qing princes. It can be established in the short term. (Seventh Dispatch)

(Peiping) The pseudo-organization in Jixian County plans to repair the original long walls of the Eastern Tombs, restoring them to their original state. They have sent many people to measure the border walls, which are thirty li long. The construction costs require 600,000 yuan. The pseudo-organization has suspended the project because the required funds are too large. (Eighth Dispatch)

Terror of Great Floods Strikes Again; Luan River and Yongding River Both Swell; Yellow River Water Level Rising Daily; Xiang River Breaches Dyke, Qianjiang Issues Emergency 6

(Peiping) Due to continuous heavy rains in the Xuanhua and Huailai areas upstream, the Yongding River has seen mountain torrents. At 5:00 AM yesterday, the water level gauge at the Huitong Temple measuring station north of Lugou Bridge rose sharply from over eleven feet to sixteen feet. Men Zhenzhong, the director of the River Affairs Bureau, immediately telegraphed the river banks along the river to strictly defend. This morning, the water level continued to rise. At 5:00 PM, it rose to 17 Hua feet. Jinmen Gate and all the arches of the Lugou Bridge were submerged, and the currents were extremely turbulent. (Eighth Dispatch)

(Peiping) The Luan River's water level has risen sharply, and the water level is only two feet away from the embankment. The Luan River bridge on the Peiping-Mukden Railway is in danger. The engineering section has been sending workers to inspect and prevent damage for several days. (Eighth Dispatch)

(Peiping) The Yongding River's water level rose sharply by sixteen feet today due to a flash flood upstream. (Seventh Dispatch)

(Tientsin) Due to more than ten days of rain in Jixian County, the Qingdianwa Tai River in the county has been flooded and has overflowed. More than ninety villages in the fifth and seventh districts have been affected by the flood, and more than a thousand acres of crops have been destroyed. Traffic in all villages has been cut off. The county magistrate has telegraphed the province for relief. (Eighth Dispatch)

(Hankou) Deng Bing, the magistrate of Qianjiang County, urgently telegraphed the provincial government, saying that the Xiang River continued to rise. On the 6th, it poured into the levee, and the Meijiazui area was overwhelmed before it could be rescued. Within a few hours, dozens of miles to the southeast became a waterlogged area. The rescue of the forts is still not out of danger, and there are many leaks and collapses in other low-lying areas. He is supervising the emergency rescue and requests an early emergency account to save the refugees. (Eighth Dispatch)

(Kaifeng) On the night of the 7th, the Yellow River at Tongguan rose by eight Gongcun. On the 8th, the Yellow River at Shaanxi rose by three meters and four centimeters. (Eighth Dispatch)

(Peiping) News, the Luan River's water level has risen sharply since the evening of the 7th, with the water level only two feet away from the embankment. The River Affairs Bureau has sent personnel to strictly guard against it. Also, the Yongding River's water level has risen sharply, and the current is very rapid along the downstream coast. If it rises further, it will greatly affect the power plant of the Shijingshan Electric Light Company in western Peiping. (Eighth Dispatch from Central News Agency)

(Jinan) This morning, the River Bureau received a telegram from the Shaanxi station, stating that the water level was 292.52 meters, an increase of 1.32 meters compared to the 2nd. A follow-up telegram stated that it had risen another 0.54 Gongcun. The Bureau specially telegraphed the heads of all sections of the river to strengthen prevention. (Eighth Dispatch)

(Hankou) The water level of the Yangtze River was stable on the 8th. The Sichuan-Yichang section retreated on the 5th, while the Changsha-Yueyang section rose on the 5th. The Xiang River also showed a trend of receding. Several more sections of the Hanchuan People's Fort collapsed. Telegraphic communication between Yueyang and Hankou is disrupted. (Eighth Dispatch)

Kung Hsiang-hsi Arrives in Taiyuan Yesterday 7

(Taiyuan) Kung Hsiang-hsi stayed in Taigu for several days due to the rain. He arrived in Taiyuan at noon on the 8th. Important figures held a banquet in the evening. He is scheduled to meet with Yan Xishan at the riverside on the 9th, fly to Xi'an on the 10th, and fly to Kaifeng on the 12th, returning to Nanjing within a week. (Eighth Dispatch)

(Taiyuan) Kung Hsiang-hsi stayed in his ancestral home of Taigu for several days due to the rain. He arrived in Taiyuan by car at 7:00 PM on the 8th. He plans to go to the riverside to meet Yan Xishan on the morning of the 9th. He will fly to Shaanxi to meet Shao Lizhi on the morning of the 10th. A Junkers aircraft flew from Peiping to Taiyuan on the afternoon of the 8th for standby. (Eighth Dispatch from Central News Agency)

(Taiyuan) Kung Hsiang-hsi has not yet arrived in Taiyuan due to continuous heavy rains in Taigu and the car being blocked. There is still no definite news as to when he will arrive. The Central Government has telegraphed him to return to Nanjing before the 10th. Kung telegraphed Shao Lizhi, Chairman of Shaanxi, this morning, saying that he would fly to Shaanxi one or two days after meeting with Yan Xishan. A Junkers aircraft is scheduled to fly from Peiping to Taiyuan on the 8th. The seven members of Kung's entourage to Shaanxi have been determined. The rest and their families will take the Zhengtai train south. A special car has been prepared for them at the Shijiazhuang station. (Eighth Dispatch)

(Peiping) Zhao Pilian arrived in Peiping from Tianjin this afternoon. After visiting He, he will return to Taiyuan within a few days and go to Heping Village to visit Yan's illness and report on the situation in Nanjing. He will return to Nanjing in one or two months. (Seventh Dispatch)

Xu Yongchang and Others Arrive in Nanjing to Report on the Military and Political Situation in Shanxi Province 8

(Nanjing) Xu Yongchang, Chairman of Shanxi Province, accompanied by Yang Aiyuan, commander of the army, Jing Yuexiu, commander of the division, and more than 20 secretaries, arrived in Nanjing by Gonghe boat from Wuhan on the afternoon of the 8th. Xu said that he came here to report to the Central Government on the military and political situation in Shanxi Province. After staying for two or three days, he will take a boat to Jiangxi to report to Chiang Kai-shek. (Eighth Dispatch)

(Nanjing) Xu Yongchang, Yang Aiyuan, Jing Yuexiu, and their entourage, traveled east on the Jianghe ship of the Jardine Matheson Company on the evening of the 6th and arrived in Nanjing at 11:30 AM on the 8th. Li Hongwen, representative of the Shanxi Provincial Government in Nanjing, Wang Yongbin, Chairman of the Examination Committee, and all the staff of the Shanxi Provincial Government's office in Nanjing, totaling more than 20 people, went to the Jiangbian Wharf to greet them. After the ship docked, Xu and others disembarked and took cars into the city to rest at the hotel. It is reported that Xu and others came here to report to the government authorities on the recent military and political situation in Shanxi Province. After completing their affairs in Nanjing, they will go to Jiangxi to meet with Chairman Chiang Kai-shek for instructions. (Eighth Dispatch from Central News Agency)

(Nanjing) Xu Yongchang, Yang Aiyuan, Jing Yuexiu, and several members of their entourage arrived in Nanjing on the Jianghe ship at around 11:00 AM on the 8th. After arriving at the hotel, they visited friends in the afternoon. They plan to visit the mausoleum on the morning of the 9th. Yang Aiyuan, on behalf of Xu, told reporters that we have not met with the central authorities for a long time, so we came to Nanjing to receive instructions and report on the military and political situation in Shanxi Province. We plan to stay in Nanjing for three or four days. After reporting to the officials, we will go to Xunyang to meet with Chairman Chiang Kai-shek. The recent situation in Shanxi Province that can be reported is as follows: (1) In terms of military affairs, due to the lack of military spending, the army has been reduced. The original infantry, cavalry, and artillery in Shanxi and Suiyuan provinces totaled nine divisions, but they were based on a four-company system. Now, after the reorganization conference, it has been decided to reduce one company per battalion and adopt a three-three system. 20,000-30,000 officers and soldiers have been reduced, saving 200,000 yuan in salaries. The reorganization will be completed before August 1st and the new system will be implemented. The officers and soldiers who were laid off this time will be given one month's severance pay. (2) In terms of politics and government, due to financial difficulties, new policies cannot be implemented. The province's income, including national taxes allocated by the central government, totals about one million yuan per month, which is only enough to maintain government expenses. All construction is unlikely to be carried out. Only the Datong-Puzhou Railway is being actively built. The Jiexiu section has been opened to traffic. By the end of the year, two-thirds of the entire line may be completed, and the entire line will be completed by the spring of next year. (Eighth Dispatch from Central News Agency)

Fellow Townsmen from Hunan in Nanjing Welcome He Jian Yesterday; Central National Arts Hall Also Holds Welcome Reception 9

(Nanjing) Fellow townsmen from Hunan in Nanjing held a welcome reception for He Jian at the YMCA on the 8th. Also, the Central National Arts Hall held a welcome reception on the 8th, as He Jian strongly promoted national arts in Hunan, and performed national arts. (Eighth Dispatch)

(Nanjing) He Jian will fly to Jiangxi on the morning of the 10th after completing his official duties in Nanjing to participate in the opening ceremony of the Lushan Military Officers Training Corps. His entourage, including Ling Zhang, director of the office, and Zhang Muxian, director of the accounting department, will take a boat to Jiangxi this morning to wait for He to return to Hunan together. (Eighth Dispatch)

Executive Yuan, Together with Various Ministries, Reviews Total Amount of Debt 10

(Nanjing) The Executive Yuan, together with the Ministries of Finance, Communications, Railways, etc., is reviewing the total amount of debt and its types. After deciding on repayment methods, they will negotiate with the creditor groups to reorganize them separately. It is reported that the total amount of unsecured foreign debt is about 1 billion yuan, of which about 35% belongs to Japan, totaling 362.15 million Japanese yen. It is reported that the Japanese creditors have formed a creditor group and plan to send representatives to China to negotiate. (Eighth Dispatch)

Ministry of Finance Negotiating Implementation of Business Tax on Foreign Merchants 11

(Nanjing) The Ministry of Finance is negotiating with the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to implement the business tax on foreign merchants because the regulations for business tax on foreign merchants in China have not been established, and they have not been collected. They plan to formulate improved business tax measures, consult with the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, and levy business tax on foreign merchants in accordance with the law to maintain the business of Chinese merchants and increase tax revenue. (Eighth Dispatch)

All Supervisory Committee Members Strive for Disciplinary Power 12

Please Amend the Organization Law of the Yuan

(Nanjing) A member of the Supervisory Yuan said that all members of the Yuan plan to submit a request to the President to ask the National Government to amend the Yuan's organization law to increase disciplinary powers so that cases can be handed over for disciplinary action after impeachment, so that corrupt officials will know how to restrain themselves and the supervisory powers can be exercised without hindrance. (Eighth Dispatch)

China National Aviation Corporation Prepares to Restore Shanghai-Guangdong Air Route 13

(Nanjing) China National Aviation Corporation has ordered two new large aircraft from the United States, which will be delivered in three months and shipped to Shanghai next month. After assembly, the Shanghai-Guangdong air route will be restored. The two accidents on this route occurred near Xiangshan. For the safety of navigation, a radio direction finder has been installed near Xiangshan. Aircraft are also equipped with direction finders. In the future, when aircraft fly to Xiangshan, they will not get lost again even if they encounter heavy fog or darkness. (Eighth Dispatch)

Food Prices Soar in Capital 14

(Nanjing) Due to the drought, food prices are soaring. The Municipal Social Affairs Bureau has scheduled a discussion with rice merchants on the 11th to discuss relief and restrict price increases. (Eighth Dispatch from Central Government)

Person in Charge of Ministry of Finance Speaks on New Tariff 15

Tax Reduction on Cloth Has Little Impact on Domestic Textile Industry; Paper Relies on Foreign Supply, Tax Reduction Is to Take Care of Consumption; Hope Domestic Merchants Strive to Improve to Reduce Production Costs

(Nanjing) The person in charge of the Ministry of Finance gave a statement on the new import tariffs implemented by the Customs on the 8th. He said that the tariffs should be revised after a considerable period of implementation to suit the national conditions. As for the contents of the new tariffs, the tax reduction on cotton fabrics is limited to printed and yarn-dyed fabrics. This is not the main product of China's textile industry. Except for slight changes in Western satin damask cotton flannelette, there are no increases or decreases in the two major categories of plain and bleached cotton fabrics, which are produced the most domestically. It can be seen that the tax reduction on cloth in the new tariff has little impact on the domestic textile industry. The tax reduction on paper is the suggestion of the competent cultural authorities because paper for printing books still relies on foreign supply. The tax reduction is to take care of consumption. As for the tariff rate on fish and seafood products, there have been changes. For example, due to the strong request from overseas Chinese in Hong Kong and Macau, the tax on salted fish had to be reduced slightly. The tax on fish and seafood similar to salted fish has also been reduced, but the tax rate is still above 20% ad valorem. The import tax on cotton has been increased to maintain the rural economy. The tax rate on machinery is mostly 5% ad valorem, which was originally low. Now, a slight increase will not hinder construction. Taxes have been increased on pig iron, sulfuric acid, hydrochloric acid, calcium carbonate, iron wire yarn, rubber products, wood chips, wood shavings, tiles, porcelain, etc., which provide considerable protection for the domestic iron smelting, chemical, and match industries. It is hoped that Chinese canning factories will strive to improve technology and management to reduce production costs and compete with foreign merchants. (Eighth Dispatch from Central News Agency)

(Nanjing) The Ministry of Finance explained the tariff and responded to the opinions of the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce and various groups requesting the cancellation of the tariff rules that had been set. It believes that the Ministry of Finance's feelings regarding this amendment to the import tariff are different from the views of the business community, which proves that the Ministry of Finance has no intention of revising it at this time. (Eighth Dispatch)

Current Commentary

French Foreign Policy and Barthou's Trip to Eastern Europe 16

— Yi

France, as the protagonist of the Versailles system, has always held a commanding and freely manipulative position on the European continent. However, since the rise of Hitler, feeling the "brown danger," it has been concerned that the Versailles system might be shaken. Furthermore, in the past half-year, the relationship between Italy and Austria-Hungary has become increasingly close, making it impossible to realize the Danube Plan, which France has been working on for a long time. Recently, seeing Hitler and Mussolini meet in Venice, it fears that the Versailles system will be hit before the two enemies join hands.

On the other hand, Britain, separated from the European continent by a narrow strip of water, although also relying on the Versailles system for survival, has ignored France's exclusive control of hegemony for fifteen years. Therefore, it often adopts a policy of supporting Germany and restraining France, shuttling between Berlin and Paris. Britain's bias has further plunged France into encirclement. The verbal battle between British and French representatives at the Geneva Disarmament Conference in early June is proof that the contradictions between Britain and France are more tense than before. From this point of view, it seems that the difficulties of French diplomacy have never been as great as they are today in the past decade.

In the world, only when things become difficult do they change, and only through change can they become smooth. Since France ratified the Franco-Soviet non-aggression treaty, it has not only abandoned its traditional anti-Soviet movement, but also further strengthened friendly relations with the Soviet Union, thereby maintaining a new balance of power on the European continent. The flexibility of French diplomacy can be seen from this. Due to the improvement of Franco-Soviet relations, the satellite states of the Little Entente and Poland, under the leadership of France, have also successively reconciled with the Soviet Union. The so-called multilateral convention containing the definition of aggressor, signed by the Little Entente and Poland last July, and the simultaneous restoration of diplomatic relations between Romania and Czechoslovakia with the Soviet Union in June this year, are clearly new gains after the change in French foreign policy. With these new gains, the threats France faces on the European continent have naturally been reduced.

However, from another perspective, it seems that the satellites under the leadership of France are also showing a slight tendency to drift away. For example, Poland's closeness to Germany is one of the facts. Therefore, the current foreign policy of France, in addition to attracting the Soviet Union to join the League of Nations to strengthen its support, only has to exert its diplomatic skills to make the satellites more united around the Versailles system in order to confront the anti-Versailles system front in Europe. Barthou's previous visits to Warsaw and Prague were concrete manifestations of the aforementioned foreign policy. Recently, Barthou revisited Eastern Europe on June 18, first going to Romania, then to Yugoslavia, and returning to Paris on the 27th. His hot and dusty journey was nothing more than an attempt to use his eloquent tongue to step up the unity of the existing forces of the Versailles system in order to break through the difficulties of French diplomacy.

It is said that when Barthou's car entered Romanian territory and arrived in a city, residents in full dress came to the station to welcome him warmly, and even the Senate and House of Representatives declared Barthou an "Honorary Citizen of Romania." The welcome he received in Yugoslavia was no less warm than in Romania. We certainly do not believe what Parisian newspapers claim, "The French Foreign Minister conquered Romania in twenty-four hours." However, it can be confidently said that Barthou's trip can make the two satellites stand on the same front with France. At a meeting of the Foreign Affairs Committee of the French Chamber of Deputies on the 6th of this month, Barthou declared that the main purpose of French diplomacy is based on the principle of "seeking peace anytime, anywhere." What is peace? In Barthou's mind, it is nothing more than maintaining the balance of power under the Versailles system.

If French diplomacy really goes one step further, then the forces against the Versailles system will naturally "rise with the tide." The Hungarian demonstrations sparked by Barthou's declaration against amending the peace treaty are just one example. Is the diplomatic war of intrigue perhaps the means that must be adopted on the eve of armed conflict?

Okada Cabinet's Six Policies: Thoroughly Rectify Discipline, Actively Prepare for a Major War and the Russo-Japanese War, Similar to the Nature of the Former Katsura Cabinet, Poor Atmosphere in the Diet, Life Expectancy Likely to Be Short 17

(Tokyo) The Okada Cabinet, due to a dispute with the Seiyukai, only completed its organization this morning. In the next Diet session, it is inevitable that it will clash head-on with the Seiyukai, but the Seiyukai itself will definitely split in the near future, so its power is not to be feared. It is rumored that the new cabinet's policy guidelines are roughly as follows:

(1) Thoroughly rectify discipline and eliminate corruption in the central and local governments. This is the purpose of appointing Ohara as Minister of Justice and Goto as Minister of Interior.

(2) Expand the army and navy and prepare for World War II. The nature of this cabinet is similar to that of the first Katsura Cabinet before the Russo-Japanese War. Before the Katsura Cabinet, the elder statesmen took turns forming cabinets, so the Katsura Cabinet was called a third-rate cabinet. Komura was in charge of foreign affairs, and Terauchi and Yamamoto, the mainstays of the army and navy, were appointed as Ministers of the Army and Navy. Okada's Minister of Foreign Affairs, Hirota, is the successor to Komura's diplomacy, and Osumi and Hayashi are also central figures in the military. Therefore, the purpose is to prepare for war. (3) Consolidate finances and administration and change to a wartime organization.

(4) Implement a colonial policy in China. The Prime Minister concurrently serves as Minister of Colonial Affairs in order to reform the system at any time.

(5) Solve the rural problem, eliminate domestic unrest, and guard against domestic revolution.

(6) Implement a tough policy and carry out diplomacy of cooperation with all nations with the determination to not hesitate to fight a war. (8th United Press)

(Tokyo) The atmosphere in the Diet is that the Okada Cabinet disregards the Diet and combines with political parties and bureaucrats to form a cabinet that touts discipline rectification, but whether the selection of personnel can meet this point is highly questionable, so the evaluation is not good. The only hope is that Minister of Agriculture and Forestry Goto will seek fairness in elections, but there is also a risk of stopping halfway. Considering these things, the Okada Cabinet is likely to be unexpectedly short-lived. (8th Special Dispatch Telegraph)

Enthronement Ceremony in the Imperial Palace 18

(Tokyo) The Okada new cabinet was completely decided only at 3:30 this morning. Okada, the new Prime Minister, entered the palace at 10:00 this morning. At 10:20, the Emperor's Appointment Ceremony for Prime Minister Okada was held first. Then, at 11:00, with Prime Minister Okada standing by, the Emperor's Appointment Ceremony for each cabinet member was held. The list of new cabinet members is as follows:

Prime Minister Okada Keisuke (Admiral of the Navy), Minister of Interior Goto Fumio (Former Minister of Agriculture and Forestry), Minister of Foreign Affairs Hirota Koki (Reappointed), Minister of the Army Hayashi Senjuro (Reappointed), Minister of the Navy Osumi Mineo (Reappointed), Minister of Finance Fujii Masanobu (Former Vice Minister of Finance), Minister of Justice Ohara Nao (Chief Judge of the Tokyo High Court), Minister of Education Matsuda Genji (Minseito), Minister of Agriculture and Forestry Yamazaki Tatsunosuke (Seiyukai), Minister of Commerce and Industry Machida Chuji (Minseito), Minister of Communications Tokonami Takejiro (Seiyukai), Minister of Railways Uchida Shinyai (Seiyukai), Minister of Colonial Affairs Okada Keisuke (Concurrently), Chief Cabinet Secretary Kawada Isao (Vice Minister of Colonial Affairs) (8th China Press)

First Cabinet Meeting Held 19

(Nanjing) After the Imperial Appointment Ceremony was completed at 11:00 this morning, Prime Minister Okada immediately convened the first cabinet meeting to determine the cabinet's policy. Prime Minister Okada then gave an oral statement on the general policy. (8th China News Agency)

(Tokyo) At 12:15 p.m. today, the Okada new cabinet held its first cabinet meeting at the Prime Minister's official residence. All cabinet members, including Prime Minister Okada, attended. The Prime Minister said in his address that he had received the great order to take charge of national affairs and hoped for the assistance of everyone. He intended to implement fair and bright politics based on the constitution, and especially to strive for the rectification of discipline. Then, after deciding on the following two items, the meeting ended at 12:45 p.m., and everyone raised champagne to celebrate the establishment of the cabinet.

(1) The cabinet meeting dates are the same as before, twice a week on Tuesdays and Fridays. (1) Government policies will be decided after consultation with the cabinet. (8th Dentsu Telegraph)

Hirota Koki Reiterates Diplomatic Aspirations, Advocates Convening a Five-Minister Conference to Make National Policy More Concrete 20

(Tokyo) After the first meeting on the 8th adjourned, Foreign Minister Hirota spoke about his aspirations regarding foreign policy as follows:

I will continue to do my best to follow the policy of cooperative diplomacy decided by the Five-Province Conference and will never change its purpose. Now that both domestic and foreign affairs are in a serious situation, I have been reappointed as Foreign Minister, and the responsibility is heavy, needless to say. As for the relationship between Japan and the United States, a general understanding has already been reached when Hull and Hirota exchanged notes, so the friendly relationship between Japan and the United States is no longer a time for talk, but has already entered a practical stage. I plan to wait for Ambassador Saito (Japanese Ambassador to the United States) to return home to hear the detailed situation and then study it. As for Sino-Japanese relations, they have gradually improved, which is a factual proof, so the policy toward China must still follow the previous policy. The recent problems in Japan-Soviet relations are expected to be resolved soon, but the Manchurian problem is the most important problem facing Japan today. Therefore, the people must do their best to devote all their efforts to it in order to make progress. In order to complete the Manchurian problem, Japan must bear the important parts of its manpower and financial resources and plan its progress with this awareness. Now the world is in a state of panic in both political and economic terms. If we want to overcome this phenomenon, it is impossible without the joint efforts of the great powers. If the great powers can feel their responsibility to maintain peace at this time and understand each other, then the seeds of the world's turmoil can be extinguished. Next year's naval conference can be said to be the greatest opportunity to achieve this goal. (8th United Press)

(Tokyo) Hirota's reappointment is conditional on continuing to maintain the national defense and diplomatic policies decided by the previous cabinet's Five-Minister Conference. Now, in order to make it more concrete, he has proposed to Prime Minister Okada that the Five-Minister Conference of Okada, Hirota, Hayashi, Osumi, and Fujii be convened as soon as possible to discuss general national defense and diplomatic policies and fundamental countermeasures for the disarmament conference. (8th Dentsu Telegraph)

Prime Minister Okada Complies with the Wishes of the Military, Striving to Realize All So-Called National Defense Policies 21

(Tokyo) Minister of the Army Hayashi's statement is as follows: It is rumored that the condition for my reappointment is to recognize the army's national defense policy, but it is not as serious as the rumors. I have fully explained my thoughts to the Prime Minister and established a considerable understanding, which is a fact. (8th Dentsu Telegraph)

(Tokyo) The army's observation of the new cabinet is that it is appropriate to establish a cabinet of this extent in light of the current situation and hopes that the Okada new cabinet will move forward based on policy. Also, Prime Minister Okada has recognized the army's important national policies, so there is considerable confidence in its implementation. Furthermore, it is determined to fully request Prime Minister Okada in the future, that is, national defense policies such as strengthening military preparations and resolving policies toward Manchuria. Especially for the latter, it wants to make the Kwantung Office a local office, change it from a three-in-one to a two-in-one based on the traditional system, establish an organization to supervise the South Manchuria Railway and other companies in Manchuria under the jurisdiction of the Ambassador Plenipotentiary, and plan to abolish the Ministry of Colonial Affairs, which is an obstacle. Also, when Minister of the Army Hayashi was reappointed, he obtained Prime Minister Okada's consent to the implementation of such policies, so its premise was that the Prime Minister concurrently served as Minister of Colonial Affairs at the time of this cabinet formation. (8th Dentsu Telegraph)

Following the Old Ways, Fujii Talks About Financial Policy 22

(Tokyo) Today, Minister of Finance Fujii stated his aspirations regarding future financial and economic policies. The main points are summarized as follows:

(1) In principle, financial and economic policies will follow the policies of former Minister of Finance Takahashi. (1) Financial management aims to reduce public bonds and save expenditures in order to achieve a balance of accounts. However, the current internal and external situation requires considerable facilities for national defense costs and others, so it will be difficult to rapidly establish finances in the future. (1) Therefore, increasing taxes is felt to be necessary, but the timing and methods of implementation must be carefully studied. That is, the harmonization of national defense, diplomacy, and finance will be carried out in the same way as the policy of the previous cabinet. (8th Dentsu Telegraph)

Rumor That the Ministry of Colonial Affairs Will Be Abolished, One Saying That Konoe Will Be Appointed Minister of Colonial Affairs 23

(Tokyo) The rumor of the abolition of the Ministry of Colonial Affairs has been very strong recently. The Okada new Prime Minister has repeatedly denied it, but he has not recommended another suitable person to serve as Minister of Colonial Affairs. Okada himself concurrently serves, but the political world expects that it will be abolished in the future. The reasons are as follows: (1) The military is in favor of abolition, believing that although the Ministry of Colonial Affairs claims to govern Taiwan, Korea, Sakhalin, the Kwantung Leased Territory, and the South Pacific Mandated Islands, these places can be governed by the Ministry of Interior, so abolishing a province can save administrative costs. (2) The immigration matters that the Ministry of Colonial Affairs has managed in the past, except for a part of South America, will focus on Manchuria in the future, so the immigration business must be managed by the military. (3) The Kwantung Leased Territory and the South Manchuria Railway Company are currently managed by the Ministry of Colonial Affairs, but this matter must be managed by the Commander of the Kwantung Army in the future. (8th China Press)

(Tokyo) The fact that the Prime Minister concurrently serves as Minister of Colonial Affairs is opposed by the military and foreign affairs due to the relationship with the policy toward Manchuria. It is a temporary concurrent appointment, and the Ministry of Colonial Affairs will be abolished at an appropriate time, but on the other hand, it is said that there is no understanding between the military and Prime Minister Oka regarding the abolition of the Ministry of Colonial Affairs. It is because they want to appoint Prince Konoe Fumimaro, who is currently returning to the United States, as Minister of Colonial Affairs. It is said to be a temporary convenience. (8th Dentsu News Agency)

Tokonami Demands to Leave the Party 24

(Tokyo) Tokonami, Yamazaki, and Uchida, who violated the Seiyukai's party resolution and decided to join the cabinet, jointly submitted an application to leave the party to the Seiyukai headquarters at 9:40 a.m. on the 8th. (8th United Press)

Signs of Division in the Seiyukai 25

(Tokyo) The Seiyukai's executive officers will expel the members of the new cabinet who joined the cabinet, both cabinet ministers and parliamentary vice-ministers, after they leave the party, or they will be expelled if they do not leave the party. However, members of the Tokonami faction may not leave the party one after another and will temporarily remain in the party, taking a self-respecting attitude. However, their self-respecting attitude is not to observe the party quietly, but to wait for the surrounding situation to be favorable to them and then make a decision. Therefore, although it will not split on the surface for the time being, the crisis of the Seiyukai is slowly proceeding from within. (8th Dentsu News Agency)

(Tokyo) The Seiyukai opened a general affairs meeting at 9:00 this morning to discuss the disciplinary action against Tokonami Takejiro, Uchida Shinyai, and Yamazaki Tatsunosuke, who joined the Okada Cabinet. As a result, it was decided that the three individuals disregarded the party's resolutions and disrupted the party's rules and were resolutely punished with expulsion. The three individuals were immediately notified, and the Seiyukai has shown signs of division at this point. (8th Dentsu News Agency)

Tsushima Internally Appointed as Vice Minister of Finance, Director of the Social Affairs Bureau Promoted to Vice Minister of Interior 26

(Tokyo) It has been internally decided that Tsushima Juichi, Director of the Financial Bureau, will be promoted to Vice Minister of Finance. It is said that Aoki Kazuo, Director of the Foreign Exchange Management Department, is most likely to be transferred to the post of Director of the Financial Bureau. (8th Dentsu Telegraph)

(Tokyo) Goto, the new Minister of Interior, has decided to promote Niwa Shichiro, Director of the Social Affairs Bureau, to be the successor to Chao, the former Vice Minister of Interior. Brief Biographies of New Cabinet Members, Average Age is Just Under Sixty 27

(Tokyo) This Okada new cabinet is somewhat fresher than the Saito era, which was called an elder cabinet. At the time of its establishment, the average age of the Saito cabinet was 63, while the new cabinet is 59.9. Their places of origin and ages are recorded on the left:

Okada Keisuke, 67 years old; Hirota Koki, 57 years old;

Page 8

Goto Fumio, 51 years old; Fujii Masanobu, 50 years old; Hayashi Senjuro, 59 years old; Osumi Mineo, 59 years old; Ohara Nao, 58 years old; Matsuda Genji, 60 years old; Yamazaki Tatsunosuke, 55 years old; Machida Chuji, 72 years old; Tokonami Takejiro, 68 years old; Uchida Shinyai, 55 years old. The youngest member of the cabinet is Minister of Finance Fujii, who is 50 years old, and the oldest is Minister of Commerce and Industry Machida, who is 72 years old. (8th United Press)

Minister of Interior Goto Fumio 28

Goto was born in Oita Prefecture in Meiji 17 (1884). He graduated from Tokyo Imperial University in Meiji 41 and immediately entered the Ministry of Interior. In Taisho 11, he was appointed Director of the Police Affairs Bureau. In Taisho 13, he was appointed Director-General of the Taiwan Governor-General's Office. In Showa 3, he was appointed Chairman of the National Youth Association. In Showa 5, he was appointed a member of the House of Peers. In Showa 7, he was appointed Minister of Agriculture and Forestry in the Saito cabinet. He is a close confidant of Izawa, the leader of the bureaucratic faction, and is also known as the protagonist of the new bureaucratic faction. He is highly valued by elder statesmen and bureaucratic factions and is the mainstay of the Okada cabinet.

Minister of Education Matsuda Genji 29

Matsuda was born in Oita Prefecture, Kyushu, in Meiji 8 (1875). After graduating from Nihon University, he became a lawyer. Since Meiji 41, he has been elected to the House of Representatives eight times. He initially belonged to the Seiyukai and served as a councillor with Imperial appointment in the cabinet and Vice-Speaker of the House of Representatives. When the Seiyukai split in Taisho 10, he changed his allegiance to the Seiyu Honto. Later, he joined the Minseito with Tokonami and others. After Tokonami withdrew from the Minseito again, Matsuda remained in the Minseito to this day. In Showa 4, he served as Minister of Colonial Affairs in the Hamaguchi cabinet. He is a famous orator in the House of Representatives.

Minister of Commerce and Industry Machida Chuji 30

Machida was born in Akita Prefecture in Bunkyu 3 (1863). After graduating from university preparatory school, he entered the Bank of Japan and then transferred to the Yamaguchi Bank as manager. From Meiji 45 to the present, he has been elected to the House of Representatives seven times. In Taisho 4, he was appointed Parliamentary Councilor of Agriculture and Commerce in the Okuma cabinet. In Taisho 14, he was appointed Minister of Agriculture in the Kato cabinet. In Showa 4, he was again appointed Minister of Agriculture in the Hamaguchi cabinet and Minister of Agriculture in the Wakatsuki cabinet. He served as president of the Hochi Shimbun and is an elder and financial expert of the Minseito. He has a lot of property and many followers. Okada used him to contact the Minseito.

Minister of Railways Uchida Shinyai 31

Born in Ibaraki Prefecture in Meiji 13 (1880), he graduated from Tokyo Higher Commercial School. He made huge profits in the shipping industry during the war. He is a fighting general of the Seiyukai and has served as Parliamentary Vice-Minister of the Navy and Parliamentary Vice-Minister of Communications.

Minister of Justice Ohara Nao 32

Born in Niigata Prefecture in Meiji 10 (1877), he graduated from Tokyo Imperial University in Meiji 35. Afterwards, he successively served as a judicial officer. In Showa 3, he was appointed Vice-Minister of Justice. In Showa 6, he was appointed Chief Prosecutor of the Tokyo High Court until now.

Minister of Communications Tokonami 33

Born in Kagoshima Prefecture in Keio 2 (1866), he graduated from Tokyo University. He served as Minister of Interior in the Hara cabinet. In Taisho 13, he first led his comrades to leave the Seiyukai and formed the Seiyu Honto, serving as its president. In Showa 4, he returned to the Seiyukai. He is the anti-eyebrow of politicians from Satsuma (Kagoshima). In Showa 6, he also served as Minister of Railways in the Inukai cabinet. He is currently an advisor to the Seiyukai. (China Press)

(London) French Foreign Minister Barthou and Navy Minister Pietri, at the invitation of the British government, will come here together tomorrow. The procedures for the talks between the two countries will depend on how long Pietri stays in Britain. If he and Foreign Minister Barthou have to return to France at the same time, then naval issues and general European political issues will be discussed at the same time. If Barthou returns to France first, Pietri can stay for a few more hours, then Barthou's talks will be limited to discussing general political issues. British people want to know France's views on naval issues. This is well known in London. As for how French naval policy is affected by Italy's shipbuilding plan, it is not yet known. What Britain is waiting for from the French representatives is to understand this point. Prospects for the German Political Situation: Papen Visits Hindenburg; This Move is of Great Importance; Hitler Declares Trust in the Sturmabteilung (SA) in Order to Stabilize Public Sentiment 37

(Berlin) Vice-Chancellor Papen has gone to Neudeck, New York, to visit President Hindenburg to discuss the current political situation. Political circles in Berlin unanimously believe that Papen's move is of great importance. (Havas dispatch, 7th)

(Berlin) Since the coup of June 30th, it has been generally believed that the position of the Hitler government has been affected. On what basis Hitler will exercise dictatorship in the future is a question that political figures are speculating about. Since the leaders of the Sturmabteilung were executed, the members of the Sturmabteilung have felt deeply uneasy. In the past two days, the National Socialist Party (Nazi) authorities have tried various methods to restore the credibility of the Sturmabteilung. Lutz, who succeeded Röhm as Chief of Staff of the Sturmabteilung, was completely unknown before the incident. Hitler intentionally appointed a second-rate figure to this position precisely to indicate a reduction in the status of the Sturmabteilung. Hess, a Minister without Portfolio who handles party affairs for Hitler, issued a declaration to stabilize public sentiment, saying that Hitler has always trusted the Sturmabteilung. All newspapers published this declaration this morning. However, how Röhm plotted his betrayal was never mentioned. According to people familiar with the Sturmabteilung's psychology, the members of the Sturmabteilung are deeply lacking in material needs. What they hope from their deceased leaders is nothing more than to convey their plight to Hitler. They have no other ambitions. Today, German newspapers also mentioned the relationship between former Chancellor Schleicher and France. This kind of fact is unbelievable, but German newspapers repeatedly mention it. If it is true, it can also be seen that the internal affairs of Germany are difficult. The general public believes that the position of Propaganda Minister Goebbels is solid, but in reality, it is not so. Goebbels exchanged telegrams with the new Chief of Staff of the Sturmabteilung, Lutz, with extremely affectionate words. Goebbels told Lutz that he always adheres to the spirit of the Sturmabteilung. The two men's telegrams were fully published in today's newspapers. Goebbels recently fiercely attacked the military and former military officers in Essen. Today, Goebbels issued a correction, expressing his apology. As a result, the weight of his recent remarks has been greatly reduced. Also, Aviation Minister Göring once claimed that "his mission has been expanded," but military leaders do not seem to fully agree with Göring's expansion of his own mission. As for Vice-Chancellor Papen's speech at the University of Marburg, it is closely related to the cause of this coup, as everyone knows. Papen is determined to clear up the doubts that foreigners have about him. It is rumored that Papen will rely on President Hindenburg to seek a swift clarification of the situation, because Hindenburg is currently the only undeniable authority in Germany. Under the same thread, we must also pay attention to one thing: the death of former Chancellor and Defense Minister General Schleicher. According to the government gazette, he committed treason. This is what people are widely rumored. When Schleicher was buried, his friend, former Chief of Staff General Hammerstein, personally went to hold the rope. This is also a matter worthy of great attention. In short, although the outcome of the June 30th coup is not yet clear, according to those who pay attention to the situation, it will soon become clear. (Havas dispatch, 7th)

Munich It was initially thought that former National Defense Army officer General Lossow and General Sesse were also killed during the Sturmabteilung mutiny last Sunday. It is now heard that they are both alive. (Reuters dispatch, 7th)

Artificial Rain: The Soviet Union's Rainmaking Bureau Successfully Experiments, But Its Cost is Not Very Economical 39

(Moscow) The Soviet Russian authorities' (Rainmaking Bureau), established last year in the cotton-growing area of Uzbekistan, which had previously reported a drought, today released its official report on its first artificial rain experiment. Professor Gitten, director of the bureau, claimed that during the field experiment, he produced torrential rain that fell on an area of ​​one and a half square kilometers for as long as forty-five minutes. The artificial rain was produced using chemical methods and dispersing a special gas to promote the condensation of moisture in the air. As a result, this prototype rain cloud was subjected to a strong electric current, which caused it to release rain. The report further stated that this experiment was indeed successful, but the cost of production is extremely uneconomical. (National News Agency dispatch, 7th)

U.S.-Japan Trade Relations 43

(Washington) The U.S. Tariff Commission, in its study of trade with Japan for the Senate, stated that U.S.-Japan commerce is very important to both countries, accounting for a large portion of each country's foreign trade. The study is intended to serve as a basis for future commercial negotiations between the two countries, stating that in 1928, Japan's exports to the United States accounted for 42% of its total, while U.S. exports to Japan accounted for 28%. In 1932, Japan's exports to the United States accounted for 32%, while U.S. exports to Japan accounted for 36%. This shows that during the economic downturn, the United States reduced its purchases from Japan, while Japan increased its imports from the United States. The United States has benefited from this situation. However, U.S. business circles have repeatedly requested the government to implement protection policies for certain Japanese goods. The Tariff Commission's research results are purely statistical and have no relation to these specific issues. Moreover, the items requested by the business community are only a small part of the goods. Matches are one of them. The United States has now levied a domestic tax on colored stem matches to enable them to compete fairly. Another item is pencils. A gentleman's agreement has been reached between Japan and the United States to limit Japan's pencil exports to the United States. Other items, such as tuna and clams, have also had their tariffs increased. There have also been many discussions about light bulbs and rubber shoes, but all of these are not the main items of trade between the two countries. The largest item is raw silk, which accounts for four-fifths of Japan's exports to the United States. U.S. imports of raw silk are exempt from tariffs, so Japanese goods accounted for 88% of imports in 1928 and 86% in 1932. However, Japan's raw silk exports to the United States were valued at US$31.8 million in 1928, but decreased to US$10.6 million in 1932. Other Japanese goods that are exempt from tariffs include tea and hides, but these have all decreased by 1932. Goods subject to tariffs include silk fabrics, porcelain, camphor, straw hats, and light bulbs. (National News Agency dispatch, 7th)

British West Indies Prohibits Imports; Japanese Goods Fill the Panama Market 44

Panama: The British West Indies, Jamaica, has banned the import of foreign goods, so the port of Cristóbal in Panama is piled high with goods rejected by Jamaica, mostly shipped from Japan, mainly textiles, and 10,000 pairs of shoes, weighing more than 5,000 tons. Young Woman Attempts Suicide in Beijing; Early Discovery Ensures Survival 71

(Nanjing) Wang Xiangling, a 27-year-old female student at the Shanghai Art College, came to Beijing last year after graduating from the school and resided at her elder brother's home. He reported the incident to the police, who investigated and found an empty bottle of tranquilizers and four suicide notes. One was addressed to her fiancé, Fu Zhifan, in Hong Kong; one to her elder brother, Yi Lian; one to her elder sister, Xiang'ai; and one to the press. General Strike Movement of U.S. Dockworkers; Authorities Accused of Abusing Force; Labor Unrest Threatens to Spread 74

San Francisco. Labor unrest of varying degrees of severity has reportedly broken out in various industrial areas of the United States. However, the conflict between dockworkers and police here, which resulted in two deaths and many injuries, has now subsided. The waterfront area resembles a military camp, with armed troops patrolling the streets. California Governor Merriam is determined to use all the means within his power to prevent a recurrence of the disturbances. Although the National Guard will not use force beyond what is necessary, they may use their bayonets and bullets if the unrest recurs. If absolutely necessary, machine guns may also be opened. The striking dockworkers are currently quiet, focusing on a general strike movement. The labor unrest has the potential to spread to Portland, where representatives of eighty labor unions have already instructed union officials to discuss a general strike plan. It is reported that labor unrest has broken out to varying degrees in Oklahoma City, Minneapolis, and Philadelphia. The issue of a general strike has now been referred to the union strategy committee, which will promote an organized movement to bring about a nationwide strike. Today, representatives from one hundred and twenty labor unions voted to support the union officials' plan and passed a strongly worded resolution denouncing the state authorities' use of force to suppress the actions of the strikers. Tacoma and Seattle are currently quiet. The port of Tacoma is gradually becoming aware of the situation and is trying to facilitate trade between Tacoma and Alaska. Strike leaders and shipping companies have reached an agreement, so Tacoma workers have started loading cargo onto four merchant ships today for shipment to Alaska. It is reported that no fewer than four hundred passengers are traveling to Alaska by ship this afternoon, and goods are being transported by special train from other places to Tacoma for transfer to Alaska in an endless stream. Merchants in Seattle are concerned that Tacoma is monopolizing Alaskan commerce and fisheries. It is expected that they will also discuss a solution with strike leaders in the next few days to quell the dispute and restore trade there. However, the situation in Tacoma is not entirely peaceful due to this agreement. It is reported that the city's business community has formed an emergency committee advocating the deployment of armed troops in the harbor to open the entire port. However, the mayor claims that he does not want to take this action because dockworkers from Seattle, Olympia, and other nearby locations have already started working in Tacoma, loading cargo onto ships bound for Alaska. (7th Reuters Dispatch)

Military and Police Cooperate to Suppress; Communist Riot in The Hague Gradually Subsides 75

Amsterdam. The city is now peaceful after riots resumed this afternoon. Military police have subdued the rioters. Authorities have banned Communist Party meetings, arrested several of its leaders, and banned the publication of Communist newspapers. Residents are not allowed to go outside between certain hours of the day and night; violators will be shot. It is reported that the disturbances have spread elsewhere. Incidents have occurred in Rotterdam, Hilversum, and Groningen, but they were quickly quelled by the military and police working together, and several people were arrested. Prime Minister Colijn and Defense Minister Dijxhoorn arrived here today to investigate the truth. (7th Reuters Dispatch)

Amsterdam. As a result of forty-eight hours of continuous fighting between Communist Party members and police here, seven people have died and more than fifty have been injured. Other locations known as Communist Party strongholds, such as the Jordaan district, have experienced riots, an event unseen in the peaceful Netherlands for many years. Communist Party members in the Jordaan district had set up barbed wire obstacles and other things. However, the police and supporting troops have cleared all obstacles from the streets. Dutch Prime Minister Colijn arrived here this afternoon to advise the public, but the situation shows no signs of easing. Riots broke out again this morning. The Communist Party's newspaper, which has been inciting public unrest for days, has now been occupied by the police, and all printing presses have been confiscated. The government has now ordered that unemployed workers who participated in the riots will no longer be eligible for public assistance. Furthermore, in order to prevent the spread of the riots, the Prime Minister has requested special powers from Parliament to dissolve the Communist Party in the country. It is said that the recent events were orchestrated by the Communist Party. The government has also added a company of grenade launchers, two hundred foot police, two hundred mounted police, and many infantry and engineers, with machine guns, stationed at the scene of the incident to suppress it. (7th National Telegram)

Japanese Police Refuse to Withdraw from Trains Between Beiping and Shenyang 76

The Number of Japanese Police Escorting the Train Increases From Seven to Eleven

Problems in the War Zone to Be Resolved After Huang Fu Returns to Beiping

Beiping correspondence: During Sino-Japanese consultations regarding security matters on the Beiping-Shenyang train line, it was decided that the Chinese side would be responsible for the section within the Great Wall, and the Japanese side would be responsible for the section outside the Great Wall. When train service began to resume on July 1, the Japanese side suddenly dispatched seven so-called "police escorts," requesting to accompany the train for protection. After the Chinese side argued based on reason, the Japanese side agreed to limit it to one week, after which they would withdraw. In the past week, the number of Japanese police escorts has actually increased from seven to eleven. In addition, they carry light machine guns and are fully armed on the train, following behind our railway police and conducting inspections. As of today (the 7th), the one-week limit has expired. When the Beiping-Shenyang train departed from Beiping at 8:45 this morning, there were still eleven Japanese police officers, armed, accompanying the train. At the same time, the second Beiping-Shenyang train arriving from Shenyang also had Japanese police following. Because Director Yin Tong of the Beiping-Ning Railway Bureau has resigned, all foreign affairs negotiations have been suspended, and no negotiations have been initiated with the Japanese side. At the same time, the Japanese side is using the excuse that safety on the line east of Tanggu is still a problem and has decided not to withdraw for the time being.

Since the bombing of the Beiping-Shenyang train at Chadian, the Railway Bureau has ordered the Tianjin Beiping-Ning Railway Police Department to strictly guard each station along the route. The Tangshan Police Section has recently dispatched police to strictly guard each station on the Tang-Yu section. Unexpectedly, on the 5th, the first Beiping-Shenyang train departing from Beiping was struck by a large rock (approximately two feet in diameter) at the Hangu train station at around 1:00 p.m., smashing two third-class train windows. One passenger suffered minor injuries. A search was conducted, but the person who threw the rock had already escaped without a trace. Currently, key locations along the line are heavily guarded. Japanese troops are guarding and inspecting passengers at each station in the section outside the Great Wall: Qiansuo, Suizhong, Lianshan Bay, Dahu Mountain, and Juliu River. As for the internal affairs of the Eastern Travel Agency, the important liquidation and business departments are controlled by the Japanese, with only the document and general affairs departments managed by the Chinese side.

Regarding the issue of abolishing the Tanggu Truce Agreement, Yin Rugeng, the administrative inspector of the Jizhou-Miyun District, and Tao Shangming, the administrative inspector of the Yu District, recently received a telegram from Huang Fu, the chairman of the Political Readjustment Committee, stating that the central government has ordered negotiations with the Japanese side to abolish the Tanggu Truce Agreement. Therefore, all problems in the war zone can be resolved as a whole, without the need for direct negotiations. As a result, all matters concerning the rotation of the security team in the war zone and the withdrawal of Japanese troops from various passes along the Great Wall have been suspended, pending Huang Fu's return to the north to negotiate the abolition of the Tanggu Agreement. Huang recently sent a telegram to the Political Readjustment Committee, stating that he will go to Shanghai from Mogan Mountain this week and is expected to return to the north in mid-month. Yin Rugeng has agreed with the Japanese side that the handover of the Eastern Tombs will be carried out before the 18th of this month and has scheduled to leave Beiping for Malanyu on the 15th. (7th)
