Japan Actively Invades Mongolia; Military and Economic Measures Proceed Simultaneously 77

Changchun Correspondence: The Japanese army is currently actively carrying out its invasion of Mongolia. In eastern Mongolia and the Xilin Gol League, they are confiscating civilian firearms, disbanding Mongolian troops, and completing the construction of the Lixi-Duolun automobile road, transporting large quantities of military equipment and ammunition. Under the pressure of their iron hooves, the people of the Xilin Gol League dare not do anything. Currently, only the western league of Inner Mongolia remains intact. If the Xilin Gol League is occupied, the gateway to the western league will be opened, and all of Inner Mongolia will belong to the Japanese. However, Inner Mongolia still has 150,000 cavalrymen, fully equipped with firearms. If there are capable and spirited generals to unify command and rigorously train them, it may not be impossible to resist. The people of Inner Mongolia also share a common hatred of the enemy.

In addition to military aggression in western Mongolia, the Japanese are also using a so-called two-year plan to periodically survey the mineral, commercial, agricultural, aquatic, hunting, pastoral, and industrial resources, as well as the distribution, types, quantities, and nature of commercial transactions in northern Mongolia and Xing'an, attempting to establish the fundamental direction and foundation for their industrial development. They have now established a temporary industrial survey bureau with the puppet business community to formulate and implement the plan. The puppet state has agreed to provide 800,000 yuan to cover expenses. The industrial bureau survey organization is divided into three industrial and commercial classes and thirty resource survey classes, requiring a total of approximately 1,500 personnel. (Northeast News Agency)

Gansu's Diebu Prefecture Eagerly Awaits Development 78

Formerly Belonged to Us Before the Ming and Qing Dynasties

Fell to the Tubo After Repeated Warfare

Lanzhou Airmail: Approximately two hundred li southwest of Taozhou and Minxian in Gansu is a place called Diebu. Before the Ming and Qing dynasties, it was within our territory, and was a zhou (prefecture) along with Taozhou and Minxian, i.e., the four zhou of Tao, Min, Die, and Dang, as described in history. Later, after repeated warfare, it fell to the Tubo. Taozhou and Minxian were soon restored, but Diebu, because it was slightly out of the way and easily became remote, ended up being overlooked. It is said that the eastern border of this place is Taozhou and Minxian, the southern border is the Sichuan frontier, the western border is former Tibet, and the northern border is Qinghai. The soil is fertile, the climate is warm, the forests are lush, and the rivers wind around. Currently, many people from Lintao, Minxian, Linxia, Zhang, and Long counties go to this place to cut wood and collect medicinal herbs, and they all reap substantial profits. An investigation of the conditions in this place is as follows:

(1) People: Starting from Houguo'an, the people in each village are sparse and by nature ignorant. They all make a living by farming. More indigenous Tubo people from the upper and lower temples are harbored. There are more than two hundred monks in the temples. Many merchants from Lintan trade here. Dihasi Temple is also inhabited by indigenous people and has a church, and the missionaries are all British. The rest graze livestock in search of water and grass and rarely have villages.

(2) Land: The eastern border is Taozhou and Minxian, the southern border is the Sichuan frontier, the western border is former Tibet, and the northern border is Qinghai. The mountains surrounding it on all sides are cliffs, making it a natural and secure place. The mountain roads in places such as Luoda Mountain, Jianzang Mao Ya Ya, etc., are rugged. The area harboring the upper and lower temples to Ni'elu is slightly flatter. The land in Zhaozigou is fertile and flat, and there are hundreds of qing (unit of area) that can be reclaimed as paddy fields in the dam. There are many plains on both banks of the Baishui River, and seven or eight places like Zhaozigou can be opened as paddy fields by diverting canals for irrigation.

(3) Jurisdiction: Diebu is mostly a Fan (Tibetan) tribe. The indigenous people are scattered and graze livestock in search of water and grass. There are no special administrative organs.

(4) Climate: From Luoda to Wocang Temple, the climate is mild. Summer wheat is harvested before Xiaoshu (Minor Heat). From Wocang Temple to Diebu, summer wheat is harvested after Dashu (Major Heat). The climate from Diebu to Lamu Temple and above is slightly cold. The land is mostly flat and suitable for highland barley, oats, buckwheat, and beans. Animal husbandry is excellent.

(5) Products: All kinds of grains are produced from Luoda to Wocang Temple, and vegetables are very good, such as grapes, chili peppers, jujubes, tobacco leaves, dried persimmons, and persimmons. Cotton is especially produced. The rock salt produced from Dadagusi in Luoda is of excellent quality and taste and can also be a special product.

There are many mines along both banks of the Baishui River, and the mineral deposits are very rich. For example, at the Shangxia Gold Mines opened by the Fan people of Luota, each person can pan for more than five qian (unit of weight) of gold per day. The iron ore east of Wocang Temple often floats to the surface. The Fan people do not smelt it but can use it to make utensils. The excellence of their manufacturing can be imagined. According to the Englishman Mr. Ke, there are two mature coal mountains on the south bank of the Baishui River. Because the Fan people use pine wood for fuel, they have not been mined. If the government establishes an agency to nationalize all mineral products and use new methods for mining, then the barren land will be transformed into a zone glittering with gold. In the current state of economic decline, it would be a small supplement to the country. The grassland in this area is very wide. The Fan people all live by nomadism, so they produce many fine horses and oxen. For example, cattle and horse dealers from Taozhou and Minxian, in groups, sell cattle and horses from this place every June and July. Statistics show that more than 20,000 cattle and horses are sold to Shaanxi and Gansu each year. As for livestock such as pigs and sheep, the Fan people use them as rice and wheat for food, and the amount produced is incalculable. If the government establishes a horse farm and changes the diet to livestock, not only will there be military horses, but the tax revenue obtained will also be considerable. As for medicinal materials and furs, this place, from Tianluota to Heihe, is approximately four hundred li in length. Apart from forests, medicinal materials are produced everywhere, whether on mountains, rivers, or in valleys, such as rhubarb, dangshen, jiao, fritillaria bulbs, deer velvet, and musk, which are a major category of mountain products. Merchants from Tianjin, Wuhan, Shanxi, and Taozhou sell them to Zhongba in Sichuan and Shanyuan in Shaanxi. Taking rhubarb, dangshen, and jiao as examples, there are at least five thousand dan (unit of weight) per year. As for furs such as sheepskin, fox skin, wolf skin, leopard skin, otter skin, and gold thread velvet, the amount produced is also large. When immigrants cultivate the land, they can dig up various medicinal materials from within the cultivated land, which is truly a win-win situation.

(6) Roads: From Minxian to Guzha Road is 30 li. Going southwest along the ditch for about 10 li is Dacaotan. Going straight southwest for about 40 li to Dala Mountain, going over the mountain for 10 li to Dala Ditch, passing through villages such as Zhuliliqi Kangduojiancang, you arrive at Luoda. From Luoda, going upstream along the river, passing through Lianghekou to Deguo Temple, these temples all belong to Houyacun in Minxian. The road is very dangerous. There are two bridges here, one called Mao Ya Bridge and one called Wo Bridge. After passing the bridge, go 40 li to Womao Lower Temple. Nearby is Wocang Village, about several li away, and then there is Wocang Upper Temple. Going along the river for 60 li to Ni'e Village, and along the river into Zhaozigou, you arrive at Dihasi Temple, which is 60 li away. Dihasi Temple has a church. From Dihasi Temple to Diecheng is 30 li. From Diecheng to Lamu Temple is about 70 li. There is also a church here. The land is mostly flat and easy to travel.

(7) Rivers: The Baishui River flows in from Qinghai, runs horizontally through the middle and into Sichuan. Tributaries include small rivers such as Ni'er Cugou, Dala Gou, Hexia Gou, and Jianniu Gou, all of which flow into the Baishui River. (July 4th)

Fujian Province Divides Administrative Inspectorate Districts; District Commissioners Concurrently Serve as County Magistrates of Resident Counties; Minhou and Siming Counties Directly Under the Jurisdiction of the Department of Civil Affairs 79

Fuzhou Correspondence: Fujian Province has recently divided the province into ten administrative inspectorate districts. All commissioners, except Xu Huhu of the Second District, who is handling industrial accounts in Fuding in eastern Fujian, are in Nanchang: Wang Boqiu of the Second District, Tang Yintang of the Third District, Meng Ping of the Fourth District, Yang Yongbin of the Fifth District, Zhu Xi of the Sixth District, Chen Zhuoru of the Seventh District, Lin Sixian of the Eighth District, Qin Zhenfu of the Ninth District, and Sheng Kaidi of the Tenth District. Around the 15th of this month, they will transfer from Jiangxi to Shanghai and then come to Fujian to be sworn in. After taking office, they will go to their respective resident counties to establish offices and work. All administrative commissioners concurrently serve as county magistrates of the resident counties, so the commissioner's office and the county government are located in the same place. All section chiefs and secretaries concurrently serve in both positions. The commissioner's office only has six staff members, eight employees, and two technicians. The cost is subsidized by the Nanchang camp at 2,000 yuan per month, and the provincial government pays 1,000 yuan per month (that is, the funds of the current four security branch offices in the east, west, north, and south districts will be reduced and transferred for use). The most important duties of the commissioners are to revitalize the countryside, organize rural militias, prohibit drugs, and suppress local bullies. The counties under the jurisdiction of each district have also been delineated as follows: The First District governs eight counties: Changle, Gutian, Pingtan, Minqing, Lianjiang, Luoyuan, Yongtai, and Fuqing, and is stationed in Changle. The Second District governs six counties: Fu'an, Xiapu, Fuding, Ningde, Shouning, and Pingnan, and is stationed in Fu'an. The Third District governs six counties: Nanping, Jiangle, Shaxian, Shunchang, Youxi, and Yong'an, and is stationed in Nanping. The Fourth District governs five counties: Xianyou, Putian, Yongchun, Dehua, and Datian, and is stationed in Xianyou. The Fifth District governs five counties: Tongan, Anxi, Jinjiang, Hui'an, and Nan'an, and is stationed in Tongan. The Sixth District governs six counties: Zhangpu, Changtai, Haicheng, Yunxiao, Zhao'an, and Longxi, and is stationed in Zhangpu. The Seventh District governs five counties: Longyan, Ningyang, Zhangping, Nanjing, and Pinghe, and is stationed in Longyan. The Eighth District governs five counties: Yongding, Changting, Shanghang, Wuping, and Liancheng, and is stationed in Yongding. The Ninth District governs six counties: Shaowu, Jianning, Taining, Ninghua, Mingxi, and Qingliu, and is stationed in Shaowu. The Tenth District governs six counties: Pucheng, Chong'an, Jianyang, Jian'ou, Songxi, and Zhenghe, and is stationed in Pucheng. Only Minhou and Siming counties, one being the provincial capital and the other being a commercial port, are directly under the jurisdiction of the Department of Civil Affairs and are not within the administrative inspectorate area. (4th)

Drought and Famine in Various Counties in Southern Anhui 80

The Second District Commissioner Establishes a New Wuhu

Wuhu News: Since the beginning of summer, the counties in southern Anhui have not received any rain, and the weather has been extremely hot and dry. The temperature is consistently above 100 degrees, and even indoors it is between 98 and 99 degrees. There is no wind at all, making it impossible to cool down. The mountain villages of Wuhu, Yicheng, Nanling, Ningguo, Tongling, Qingyang, Guichi, and Tongcheng are all suffering from drought. Ponds have dried up, and the land has cracked. The farmland in each county is no less than several million mu (unit of area), and rice and grain harvested in the autumn are the only products. During this hot summer, irrigation is needed, but there is little water, making transport difficult. Prayers for rain are everywhere, and the signs of drought and famine have already formed. Farmers are fearful all day long, and the rural economy has long been bankrupt. Few families have accumulated food. If the autumn harvest is indeed hopeless, the impact is difficult to predict. Therefore, rice prices have been rising steadily in recent days. The market prices of all types of rice have risen by several qian (unit of currency) per shi (unit of volume). First-grade rice costs 4 liang and 9 qian and 5 fen (unit of weight), second-grade costs 4 liang and 8 qian and 3 fen, and the next grade costs 4 liang and 7 qian and 5 fen. Rice from river milling in prefectures costs from 4 liang and 5 qian and 2 fen to 4 liang and 8 fen. Prices are expected to continue to rise in the future, as the number of sellers is gradually decreasing. Wang Zhuren, the administrative commissioner of the Second District of Anhui and concurrently the magistrate of Wuhu County, believes that the rice market in Anhui has always been concentrated in Wuhu, which is the center of Anhui's business community. The Wuhu-Tunxi and Nanjing-Wuhu highways have recently opened, and the Nanjing-Wuhu and Wuhu-Zha railway lines are under construction. With seamless transportation, commerce, travel, and military affairs are gradually becoming the hub of the Yangtze River. However, the construction of the city cannot be compared to Nanjing and Shanghai, and even compared to Xunzhen and other places, it is inferior. In order to build a ring road around the city, a road along the river wharf, and to revitalize the market from Beiping Road to the railway station area, approximately 500,000 yuan is needed. A plan has been prepared and submitted to Chairman Chiang Kai-shek, the Anhui Provincial Government, and the Department of Construction, requesting that construction funds be increased by 50,000 to 60,000 yuan per year from this year onward to allow for step-by-step construction. (6th)

Bandits in Southern Anhui Raid Wuyuan; Troops Sent to Suppress, Bandits Flee to Chengjiashan; Liu Zhenhua Sets Deadline to Suppress Banditry in Northern Anhui 81

Wuhu Correspondence: Commander Chiang Kai-shek previously proposed that Wuyuan County in Huizhou, southern Anhui, be placed under the jurisdiction of Jiangxi Province in order to facilitate command, since it is adjacent to the Jiangxi border, allowing bandits to emerge and raid. This has already been approved by the Executive Yuan. Unexpectedly, at this time, more than a thousand bandits suddenly arrived at Kaihua Fangcun in the third district of the county. They were wearing yellow uniforms and carrying hundreds of rifles and box cannons. First, they occupied Lizhuang, looting slightly due to the poverty of the countryside and kidnapping four people for ransom, before heading to Jixi Town and causing great disturbance. No shop or resident was spared. They also kidnapped twenty-three people for ransom, before invading Zhentou. They encountered the independent platoon of the militia of the second and third districts across the river, and exchanged fire. The militia, outnumbered, was forced to retreat to the entrance of Yongyuan Village. The bandits finally rushed into Jiangwan Town at night, causing an uproar, with miserable cries shaking the sky. People fled, carrying the old and the young, climbing over mountains. The next morning, as a unit of infantry from the 272nd Regiment of the 55th Division arrived, the bandits began to retreat to their old nest in Xinjian in the tenth district of Dexing. At the same time, a large group of bandits also raided Qimen County from the Fubian area, first disturbing the 24th district before approaching the city gates, setting fires and looting before fleeing towards Chengjiashan. It is reported that two regiments of provincial troops have arrived in the western township of the county, so morale has stabilized somewhat. The county governments have reported to headquarters, requesting the dispatch of large forces to encircle and suppress the bandits to prevent them from spreading.

Liu Zhenhua, the commander of the joint suppression of bandits in the border area of the three provinces of Henan, Hubei, and Anhui, believes that banditry in various counties in northern Anhui has not been eradicated. Now that the green gauze screens have risen, he has decided to take the opportunity to set a deadline of two months to suppress the bandits. (7th)

Xiamen Bandits Rob Two Money Shops 82

Robbed of Over a Thousand Several Hundred Yuan, All Shops Closed for One Day

General Chamber of Commerce and Money Trade Associations Set Deadline for Public Security Bureau to Solve Case

Xiamen Correspondence: Recently, the situation in Xiamen has been unstable, with bandits appearing from time to time. On the afternoon of the 2nd, at 2 PM, two money shops on Datie Road were robbed simultaneously at the same location. Afterwards, all the bandits escaped, leading to the closure of all money shops in the city for one day. The Chamber of Commerce has set a deadline to solve the case, causing a significant reaction. As of today, the case has not been solved. On the afternoon of the 2nd, at 2 PM sharp, the city's money shops were in full operation, and it was a Monday, so the amount of money being received was even higher than usual. Four men wearing white silk and black Xiangyun gauze shirts and pants suddenly came to Yongkang Exchange Money Shop at No. 27 Datie Street. One of them presented 20 silver dollars and 12.4 yuan in small coins to exchange for 30 yuan in banknotes. The owner's younger brother, Su Guanghan, accepted the money and exchanged it for banknotes. Unexpectedly, the man suddenly approached Su and pointed a gun at his chest, forcing him to hand over the safe key. The other three bandits, two of whom went inside to rob, one guarded the front and side doors, and the other cut the telephone line to monitor the staff. One bandit outside the door held a Mauser pistol to watch for any wind. Passersby and neighbors thought it was police officers conducting a raid, so many stopped to watch. They then saw the bandits take the money from the wooden safe. The bandit guarding the door scattered the silver dollars in the middle of the street. The crowd then realized that it was a robbery and dispersed. At the same time, at Longyi Money Shop at No. 126 Datie Street, diagonally across from Yongkang, three men also wearing white silk and black Xiangyun gauze shirts and pants arrived. One of them, wearing ink-colored crystal glasses, presented 11.21 yuan in small coins to exchange for 9 silver dollars. After the shop assistant, Lu Jinlong, made the exchange, the bandit then presented 21 silver dollars to exchange for banknotes. When Lu was about to hand over the money, the bandit suddenly pulled out a gun and pointed it at Lu, ordering him to hand over the money safe key. Lu was terrified and ran away, exiting the rear door into Shi Lane to call for help. The bandits then entered the safe to search and rob the money. The other two bandits also entered, all with guns. One guarded the telephone, and one stood outside the door. However, since the staff at Longyi had already escaped through the rear door, the bandits did not dare to stay for long. They hurriedly searched and were about to sort the two thousand yuan in stamped silver that Hengchang had sent over, as well as the 594 yuan in stamped silver that Dingchang Money Shop had sent over, all of which were placed on the counter. The bandits then poured all the stamped silver into the street. For a moment, the clanging sound filled the air, and the street was covered in silver. The three bandits then retreated. The four bandits from Yongkang also retreated into the street at the same time. The two groups of bandits converged and fled towards Wangye Temple at the beginning of Datie Road. In front of Haifeng Trading Company, about 20 steps away from Yongkang Longyi, the bandits turned around and fired more than ten shots as a warning. Two holes were made in the Haifeng signboard, one hole in the Jinshengchang Inn signboard, three bullets hit the walls of the shops, and three bullets hit the ground. Chen Tian, the owner of Xielong in the same street, was hit by a bullet in his crotch, with two holes piercing through the front and back of his trousers. Fortunately, he was not injured. A police officer on duty nearby heard the shots and rushed to the scene, but the bandits had already fled. Because he was unarmed, he only dared to follow them at a distance and was unable to catch them, so they all escaped. The entire incident lasted only five minutes. Afterwards, an inspection revealed that Yongkang Su Tianhan's safe key was missing and had not been handed over. Lu Jinlong from Longyi had escaped, and the safe had not been opened. Only the wooden safes were searched. The bandits only took a small amount of cash. Yongkang was robbed of 813.6 silver dollars, and Longyi was robbed of 516 silver dollars, 301 yuan in paper money, 52.3 yuan in small coins, and one 5-yuan Japanese gold ticket, totaling over 900 yuan. The two shops were robbed of over 1700 yuan in total. After this incident occurred, all the money shops in the city immediately closed. At 3 PM, the Money Shops Association held an emergency meeting, which all the shops attended. As a result, representatives were sent to the General Chamber of Commerce to request that they go to the Public Security Bureau to urge a strict investigation. The General Chamber of Commerce convened an emergency joint meeting of directors and supervisors at 4 PM, which all the money shops attended. It was resolved (regarding the case on this afternoon at 2 PM, bandits robbed Yongkang and Longyi Money Shops on Datie Road simultaneously in broad daylight on a main thoroughfare, setting a new record for robbery cases in Xiamen's history, greatly harming local security and commerce, it was resolved to request the Public Security Bureau to solve the case within three days and severely punish the perpetrators according to the regulations for punishing bandits. Otherwise, merchants will have no protection and will be unable to do business. A general meeting should be convened to properly discuss solutions). As for all the money shops in the city, they will temporarily resume normal business from the 3rd, while awaiting the handling of this case. On the one hand, a telegram was sent to Public Security Bureau Chief Wang Gupan to attend a meeting to discuss the matter. Wang sent Chief Inspector Lin Tinggan to the Chamber of Commerce to express that the Public Security Bureau had ordered the detective team to solve the case within a time limit. At the same time, the Second Sub-Bureau reported that they had seen the bandits enter the tea and gambling house opposite Hefuqing on Ci Street. They then cooperated with the Japanese consulate staff to search and arrest them, while surrounding the area near Ci Street. However, after a long time, nothing was found. The case is now under control. Please allow the money shops to resume normal business so that the Public Security Bureau can focus on handling this case, etc. As of the 5th, the three-day deadline had passed, and there was still no trace of the bandits. The General Chamber of Commerce, in response to the Money Shops Association, convened a joint meeting of directors and supervisors, resolving to send Chairman Hong Xiaochun to the Public Security Bureau on the 6th to urge a speedy resolution of the case, with a deadline of the 9th. If the case cannot be solved by then, a general meeting will be convened to resolve the matter. Until the matter is resolved, all money shops will continue to operate as usual. Therefore, this case is still in a serious state. (6th)

Northwest Inspection Notes - Special Correspondent Geng Ya for This Newspaper 83

Small Dam and Big Dam

On the 22nd, at 3 AM, we departed Wang Hong Fort. In the faint morning light, the car sped past the Ning Shuo county government. Only a few simple houses were visible, along with a screen wall, earthen roofs and earthen walls, with the doors and walls slightly whitewashed. A postal worker driving a donkey passed me. I got out of the car and walked with him, talking. According to him, he had been a postal worker for ten years, earning over twenty yuan a month, and had never been in arrears. However, as he was getting older, he was deeply afraid of being dismissed. He lived in Da Ba, where his wife and children farmed. They cultivated ten mu of land themselves, yielding five shi of wheat, worth 150 yuan. After paying the Qing Xiang fee of 25 yuan, the labor levy for dam construction of 10 yuan, and grain of two shi and four dou, totaling 72 yuan, only 43 yuan remained. This was barely enough to cover the costs of tools and fertilizer. However, when faced with miscellaneous levies and disasters, they were often at risk of freezing and starvation. When asked if he grew tobacco, he replied that growing tobacco required superior land, good fertilizer, and a large amount of capital, which he had nowhere to borrow. Moreover, it was easy to be stolen at harvest time, so he usually did not grow it. However, even if he did not grow tobacco, the Qing Xiang fee still had to be paid. According to statistics, Ning Shuo County should pay a Qing Xiang fee of 350,000 yuan this year, starting from May 1st for a period of five months, with 30% to be collected by the end of June, another collection by the end of August, and the full amount collected by the end of this month. The county has 181,200 mu of land. The land that was affected by the disaster last year is still difficult to cultivate this year and should be removed from the calculation, totaling over 24,040 mu. The actual area is 157,150 mu. According to the amount, each mu should pay 2 yuan, 2 jiao, 2 fen, 7 li, 2 hao. In addition, there are additional district fees, the amount of which has not yet been determined, but it is feared that it will be at least above the 2 yuan and 5 jiao collected last year. In Hedong Jinji County, each mu is levied over 3 yuan and 3 jiao. In addition to collecting the exact amount, the collectors also forcibly take a tip of four or five jiao (the county servants who collect grain often have no salary). If they are not given the tip, they will drag away bedding and clothes.

Fifteen li (Huinong Canal Office). The fort is built like a square city, with slogans pasted on the walls such as "Welcome Chairman Song to Develop the Northwest with Economic Strength" and "The Qinghai Army is the Living Buddha of the Northwest". A rustic old man digging vegetables on the canal embankment seemed to suspect that we were officials (those in Western clothes were traveling together). He cupped his hands and asked, "Are you traveling with Song?" He then muttered to himself, "One or two days before Song was scheduled to arrive in Ning, I heard that he would inspect the big dam. The farmers and merchants along the way who could provide rest stops and reception venues were told by the district and township chiefs, 'If Song asks about the people's sentiments, you can only say good things, and never say bad things, otherwise you will be punished.' When Song gave a speech at the mass welcome rally, I leaned on my walking stick and went to listen. I saw an unhappy look on Song's face, and he didn't speak much. Could it be that he noticed our people's suffering, and that the officials are too harsh and greedy, and that someone risked their lives to complain to him?" The attention of the border people to the words, deeds and expressions of important figures is such that their earnest expectations of the central government can also be faintly seen.

After traveling several li, we paralleled the Han Canal. There were rat holes in the canal banks, and swallows used them as nests. White eggs and yellow chicks could be seen by looking down. Old swallows flew towards us in groups, seemingly unafraid of people. Passing Li Jun Fort, Ye Sheng Fort, and other places, we saw two or three cemeteries. The graves were marked with soil, which was very different from the mounds of earth and tombstones in the hinterland. The Xiaoba River was sparkling with water. The canal ditches, bridges, water level, and other constructions were all suitable for the terrain. There was a pavilion on the dam called "Xi Rui", with the couplet "The pond is full of water and the spring grass is green, the sky opens and the painting is full of evening mountains". On the opposite bank of the pavilion was the "Han Yan Canal Office" and its affiliated nursery. The Dragon God Temple was also listed there. The Canal Office has an elementary school, combining science and classics. The teacher mistook the Prime Minister's will of (dedicate ourselves to revolution) into (make effort to revolutionize), and (for forty years) into (has been forty years). A certain former director of the Ning Provincial Civil Affairs Office mistakenly wrote on a registration certificate issued last year, including the Prime Minister's instruction, (what our party advocates) mistaken the "advocates" into "obeys (the principle is to follow)", mistaken the "principle" to "this". The business has been hung for a long time without realizing it, and it is almost invisible to the naked eye.

Li Jun Fort, Wang Hong Fort, Ye Sheng Fort, and other places along the way are all named after people. The canals are crisscrossed and dense as fields. The soil is fertile and the produce is abundant. The plants and trees are secluded and beautiful. Nowhere else can all of these things be found at the same time. At 3 PM, we arrived at Da Ba and stayed for the night, covering 70 li. Da Ba used to be an important hub in the Northwest. Later, due to repeated wars, it became a ruin, and the population gradually decreased. The buildings surrounding the dam include the Tang Lai Canal Office, Qing Lai Pavilion, Cang Lang Pavilion, Wen Chang Palace, Dragon King Temple, and Bull King Temple, which are magnificent. The Bull King Temple enshrines the Bull King, the Horse King, and Su Wu. The incense is usually strong. Building dams and canals, singing operas to honor the gods, attracting crowds from far and wide, and blocking the roads for the purpose. Nowadays, due to bad harvests, frequent disasters, and insufficient manpower, the incense is dwindling. There is no money to sing operas, so the stage has been demolished. The abbot talked about it with emotion.

Suzhou - Two Ships Capsized, Eighteen People Drowned 84

A rural cargo ship from Xishan Hui and a rural cargo ship from Dongzhai River, each carrying passengers and cargo, capsized when they passed the lake area of Shishan Shigong Mountain in Xishan the day before yesterday due to a sudden storm. All the passengers fell into the river. The cries for help were very tragic. At that time, because no one rescued them, eighteen people, including Tu Fugeng, drowned at the same time. Later, Chief Zhou of the Public Security Bureau of the jurisdiction sent police to salvage the bodies. Seventeen bodies were salvaged, which was also tragic.

Wujiang - Epidemic Rampant in the County 85

Since the beginning of summer, the county has experienced severe drought, and the temperature has reached over 100 degrees Fahrenheit from time to time, leading to a widespread epidemic. People die in the morning after falling ill in the evening. Most of the victims are children. Within ten days, more than forty children in the city have died from the disease. It starts with fever, followed by coma and unconsciousness. After three or four hours, they collapse and die.

Changshu - Guard Team Holds Flag-Giving Ceremony 86

The police team of the county has been ordered to reorganize into the County Guard Team. The reorganization has been completed. The team has been received by Deputy Team Leader Fan Zhengshan and reorganized into two squadrons, with intensified training. On the 12th, they will depart for Xixi to assemble and receive inspection by personnel sent by the central government. At 8 AM on the 7th, a flag-giving ceremony was held. At that time, Team Leader Lu Cengyu of Squadron 1 led all the soldiers to the county and stood in the auditorium. Deputy Team Leader Fan presented a silk military flag to the team, which was received by Team Leader Lu. After the county magistrate gave a speech, the team returned to their post. It is now known that in order to show their spirit, the team will not take boats or cars to Xixi for inspection. They will walk in stages in the morning of the 9th, arriving in Xixi after spending a night in Yangfu. They will arrive in Xixi on the 10th and are currently preparing their equipment.

Persistent Drought - County Magistrate Offers Incense to Pray for Rain 87

The county has not rained for two months, and the drought is extremely severe. Farmland cannot be sown, and there are problems with drinking water. Although there was a brief shower the day before yesterday, it only amounted to just over an inch, and the weather cooled down slightly, but it was of no benefit to agriculture. Therefore, dragon kings are still being worshipped everywhere, and prayers for rain continue. The bronze Dragon King of Sanfeng Dragon Palace was also respectfully welcomed into the city by gentry and merchants and enshrined in Huiri Temple. Many people from all walks of life have come to offer incense and prayers. County Magistrate Zhou Heng, in order to follow public opinion, also goes to worship and offer incense at 5 AM every morning. The county government also issued a notice continuing the ban on slaughter for three days. On the 7th, it was discovered that Zhang Hexing Meat Shop was selling pork privately, and the shop owner Zhang Changming was arrested and fined. However, the weather has been clear and sunny for days, and there is still no sign of rain.

Wuxi - Business Tax Bureau Increases Tax Rates 88

Since Xia Zhenlong took office as the director of the Business Tax Bureau in Wuxi, he has actively reorganized the bureau, and tax revenue has gradually improved. However, business owners have requested a reduction in tax rates due to the sluggish business climate. Recently, the tax bureau has not investigated the capital of various industries but has freely increased tax rates, harassing merchants and creating disputes. Yesterday, Jin Da Tai Sheng and other silk shops in Jiangyin Lane paid taxes according to the original amount, but the tax bureau refused to accept it. Therefore, they followed the decision made at the temporary meeting of various industries convened by the county chamber of commerce on the 25th of last month and paid the 780 yuan tax to Jiangsu Bank, separately stored. In addition, Zhuang Yuan Da Oil Factory, with a capital of 3,000, paid taxes according to the amount. Starting from the autumn of the 22nd year, the tax bureau levied taxes according to a capital of 8,000 yuan, an increase of more than double, which is really unbearable. Therefore, they also handed over the tax of 20 yuan that should be paid to the oil factory guild and transferred it to Jiangsu Bank for separate storage. At the same time, they sent a letter to the county chamber of commerce, forwarding it to the county government and the business tax bureau for investigation, to show their response.

Rumors of Rong Zongjing's Resignation 89

Rong Zongjing, a native of the county, founded flour mills, textile factories, and other factories, totaling twenty-one, with assets of over 90 million yuan. He pays more than 10,000 yuan in national taxes every day, and the annual tax revenue is over 3 million yuan. In recent days, newspapers in Shanghai and Wuxi have reported that Rong has resigned from his position as general manager due to illness and that Rong has hired Wang Yuqing, a native of the county, as general manager. The reporter believed that this matter was of great importance to the country and society, so he went to visit the Wuxi authorities of Shenxin and Maoxin factories. According to them, Rong had been ill once last year and has recently recovered. However, in order to maintain his energy and devote his full efforts to the development of various factory businesses, he hired Wang Yuqing, the former manager of Fuxin, as general manager to jointly seek development. Rong himself does not leave the company. All the rumors are fabricated by newspapers of a certain country in an attempt to sabotage China's great industry.

Changzhou - County Magistrate Cai Resigns Again to the Civil Affairs Department 90

Cai Ziping, the county magistrate of Wujin, has been in office for more than a year. He had previously resigned to the provincial department several times, but his resignation was not approved due to telegrams from local agencies and organizations requesting him to stay. It is now known that he recently claimed to be suffering from illness and intended to go to Japan and other places to inspect model counties. Taking advantage of the construction department director's telegram summoning him to the province to discuss road construction issues, he also went to the civil affairs department to meet with Director Yu Jingtang and pleaded to resign. Director Yu consoled him and urged him to reluctantly do his best. After County Magistrate Cai returned to Changzhou, it was reported that his resignation was firm and he had submitted his resignation again in order to recuperate.

Jiangyin - Spring Cocoon Collection Improvement Fee 91

The Construction Department designated Jiangyin as a sericulture improvement area. For this year's spring cocoons, an improvement fee of three yuan must be collected for each dan of dry cocoons. The entire county's cocoon factories collected over 18,000 dans of fresh cocoons. Each dan of dry cocoons is only reeled into about 290 jin, totaling 6,000 dans of dry cocoons, collecting an improvement fee of over 18,000 yuan.

Destitute in Another Village, Short-Sighted Thoughts 92

Li Xianglin, a 26-year-old man from Chongming, enlisted as a porter in the Fujian province through the county's recruitment office in June of the year before last. Because he could not bear the pain of carrying heavy loads, he escaped in February of this year. He begged all the way from Fujian and Zhejiang and arrived in Cheng on the 5th. Near Huangtian Port, he could not return home. He hanged himself from a poplar tree with his belt. He was spotted and rescued by villagers and reported to Hua Xiongzhong, the director of the First Branch of the Public Security Bureau, who gave him five silver dollars to buy a Dada steamboat ticket and sent him back to his hometown.

Nantong - Two District Chiefs Detained and Sent to the Province 93

Commissioner Wang sent by the provincial government came to Tong to meet with Special Commissioner Zheng and County Magistrate Jin and detained and sent District Chief Chen Youqi of Yu Dong District and District Chief Ding Ziyan of Yi Yu District to the province. Commissioner Wang supervised the county police team and rushed to Yu Dong to search for accomplices in the case. It is reported that the charges against Chen, Ding, and others were conspiring to murder.

Jingjiang - Important Criminal Escorted to Tong for Interrogation 94

The Jingjiang County Government captured an important bandit Zhu Ji and sent police to escort him to the Nantong District Security Command on the 7th for interrogation.

Yangzhou - Worries About the Salt Business Moving to Qu 95

Yangzhou is an important area in Jiangbei. Because of the salt industry, commerce is particularly prosperous. Since the Transportation Department moved to Qu (浦), commerce has plummeted. In addition, the rural economy is depressed. Therefore, dozens of shops in the bustling marketplace along Yuanmen Bridge and Duozi Street have closed one after another. Although the county chamber of commerce has tried to find ways to remedy the situation, it has been ineffective. It is rumored that Salt Transportation Envoy Miao recently instructed the Si'an Public Office of the county to inform the salt merchants to purchase private land in Banpu and that there are drawings to build a new village. All salt businesses will be moved to Banpu to operate. If this plan is implemented, the market in Yangzhou will be even more unbearable. Therefore, salt merchants have been hesitating about this matter in recent days.

Haimen - Luring and Selling a Wife Leads to a Murder Case 96

Ji Shenghuai, the 35-year-old son of Ji Jinchuan, a farmer from Xilin Township in the Fourth District, hired his wife Chen to Shen Duxin's family in the same village because of his family's poverty. Shen saw that Chen was somewhat attractive, so on March 18th of this year, he colluded with Shen Duxin, Shen Zejing, and others to lure and sell Chen to Chongming. After Jinchuan and his son found out, they repeatedly negotiated with Shen, but to no avail. The day before yesterday (the 5th), Jinchuan went to Shen's place to demand her return again. Unexpectedly, Shen Duxin and others scolded him and ordered many people to push Jinchuan into the river, causing him to drown. Afterwards, they bribed Township Chief Zhai Yaoting to falsely report to the District Public Security Bureau, claiming that it was a floating body, in an attempt to absolve themselves of guilt. Ji Shenghuai, whose wife was lured and sold and whose father was killed, was filled with grief and indignation. Yesterday (the 6th), he petitioned the county government to arrest the murderers and bring them to justice in order to avenge his injustice.

Drowning Deaths in River Bathing 97

Xiao Lang, the son of Lu Zuo Xiang, a villager of Ni Jia Town in the Third District, who was over ten years old, went to the river to bathe with his neighbor Chen Guozai's young son Bao Xiang yesterday (the 6th) afternoon because the weather was extremely hot. Xiao Lang, who was unfamiliar with the water, could not control himself after entering the water and sank to the bottom of the river. After a long time, he did not come up. Bao Xiang knew that something was wrong and hurried into the water to search. Unfortunately, he fell into a deep pit and also drowned. When the family found out and went to rescue them, they were floating on the surface of the river, dead.

Jiashan - Bandits Rob Merchant Ships in Qianjing Pond 98

Qianjing Pond in the county is an important route for Hangzhou-Shanghai navigation, with many merchant ships traveling to and fro. On the afternoon before yesterday, freight ships of the Zhu, Fang, and Mao families, were loading goods and heading to Shanghai when they encountered eight flat-bottomed boats. Bandits jumped out, carrying box cannons, and ordered them to stop their ships, robbing them at will. All the cash and clothes were robbed. Afterwards, a cloth ship from Huzhou Linghu owned by the Zhang family sailed past and was also intercepted. One member of the crew was killed, and about 250 silver dollars were lost.

Xiaoshan - Locust Nymphs Appear in Various Townships 99

Recently, due to the prolonged drought in the third and fourth districts of the southern township of Xiaoshan, locust nymphs have appeared, gnawing on rice seedlings and spreading rapidly. All the reeds and grass marshes have already been eaten. Recently, the villagers there are in a state of panic because of the drought, waterlogging, and insect plagues. They no longer have time to capture locust nymphs under the scorching sun and have no choice but to let nature take its course.

Wang Jingwei Returned to Beijing the Same Night After Arriving in Shanghai - Wang Said This Trip Was Exclusively for Medical Treatment, Did Not Meet Guests - Diabetes Alleviated, Will Return in Two Weeks for Treatment - Wang Agreed to Meet Gu Weijun on the 12th in Beijing 100

Executive Yuan President Wang Jingwei, accompanied by Vice Minister of Railways Zeng Zhongming, came to Shanghai by night train from Beijing the night before last at 11 PM. At around 9 AM, he invited Dr. Noel to examine his diabetes and treat it, which took an hour. Representatives from All Sectors Hold a Memorial Today - Northern Expedition Oath-Taking Memorial - All City Agencies Will Fly Flags and Take a Holiday 101

Today is the anniversary of the National Revolutionary Army's oath-taking ceremony in Guangdong for the Northern Expedition fifteen years ago. The Municipal Party Department of this city has specifically followed the central government's prescribed memorial methods and notified all sectors of the city to send representatives to participate in the memorial service at the department at 9 AM today. In addition, all agencies will fly flags to celebrate and take a day off to show their celebration. The Songhu Garrison Command, the Municipal Security Office, the Public Security Bureau, and the police stations of the two concessions are deeply concerned that reactionary elements may take advantage of the opportunity to cause unrest and are implementing strict security measures. The Municipal Executive Committee, in addition to appointing member Tao Baichuan as the chairman of the meeting and other venue staff, also issued a proclamation to the people, saying,

Huang Fu Will Return North Soon - Will Come Down the Mountain Around the 20th, Arrive in Shanghai from Hangzhou - Then Transfer to Ping to Negotiate on the War Zone 102

Hu Shize Went to Ping Yesterday - Mayor Wu Hosted a Dinner for Gu Weijun 103

Chinese Ambassador to France Gu Weijun and Ambassador to Switzerland Hu Shize returned to the country from overseas the day before yesterday morning. Gu plans to rest in Shanghai for three to five days, then go to Jiangxi via Beijing to meet Chairman Jiang and report on the situation of the foreign affairs and international relations with China. Yesterday evening, Shanghai Mayor Wu Tiecheng hosted a dinner for Gu at his private residence on Haig Road to welcome him. Yu Zuoting, chairman of the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, as well as Wang Xiaolai, Yu Qiaqing, and others participated. As for Ambassador Hu Shize, because his father passed away in November of last year and his coffin is in Ping, he took the Ping-Shanghai joint transportation car north with his wife at 4 PM yesterday to move the coffin south and return to his hometown of Huzhou for burial. Therefore, after completing his personal affairs at the end of this month, he will still return to Shanghai and is scheduled to take the Italian ship back to his post on the 9th of next month. In addition, Shi Zhaokui, the first secretary of the Chinese Embassy in France, returned to Yangzhou yesterday morning to visit his family.

Wang Delin's Guerrilla Commander, Li Yanlu, Arrives in Shanghai, Visits Li Du and Families at the Reception Center, and Departs for Guangdong to Report on the Military Situation in the Northeast to Wang 104

Datong News Agency reports: Li Yanlu, chief of staff and guerrilla commander of General Wang Delin of the Northeast Anti-Japanese Volunteer Army, recently disguised himself, boarded the Ping-Shen train, and entered the pass to arrive in Shanghai. A Datong News Agency reporter met with him yesterday morning at a certain location. Mr. Li, besides having already visited the reception center for the families of the Volunteer Army on Julai Road and offering comfort to the received families, will take a boat to Guangdong in the next few days to personally report the military situation on the front lines to General Wang Delin. The Datong News Agency reporter specially records his statements and extracts the war reports he carried, as follows:

Lamenting the Decline of Public Morale Within the Pass 105

According to Mr. Li, "This time, when I boarded the Ping-Shen train to enter the pass, although the time required was not as long as before, which required detours, it was indeed more convenient, but also inevitably dangerous. Moreover, since the road has been closed for a long time, it is even more profound that I was able to board the train and enter the pass. The Northeast Anti-Japanese Volunteer Army has not relaxed its determination to resist, but recently, observing the public morale within the pass, it seems to be more depressed than before." Mr. Li continued, "The enemy's atrocities in the Northeast can be described as intensified. They are especially cruel to young intellectuals who are unwilling to be enslaved, even using iron wires to pierce their palms and hanging them from treetops, or pumping air into their anuses (or vaginas for women) to make their bellies bulge and then throwing them to their deaths. Such tragic situations will surely be dismissed by countrymen as alarmist talk, but how can they know that there is indeed another world outside the pass?"

Visiting Li Du Before Departing for Guangdong 106

Mr. Li also said, "My mission in entering the pass is to report the recent military situation outside the pass to General Wang Delin. Since arriving in Shanghai, I have already visited the reception center for the families of the Volunteer Army to inspect and offer condolences. I now know that General Li Zhichu is also in Shanghai, so I will also pay him a visit. In the next few days, I will take a boat from Shanghai to Guangdong to report everything to General Wang Delin." The Datong News Agency reporter now excerpts the two most recent battles in his report to General Wang Delin, as follows:

Battle of Chenjia Ridge, Muling County 107

Chenjia Ridge Station, Muling County, is the garrison of the 18th Regiment of the puppet army, led by Regiment Commander Pei (formerly Battalion Commander Pei in Yanji). On May 3, Chen Rongjiu, commander of the 8th Detachment of our army's guerrillas, led his troops to attack the station. At 12:00 PM, they advanced in three detachments, first surrounding the puppet army's regimental headquarters and cutting off the telegraph lines. They fought fiercely until dawn before retreating. Before the attack, a special service company was temporarily dispatched to collect grain, cloth, and other items, obtaining 97 bags of Japanese-made flour, two Korean cars of rice (about 10+ dan), more than 100 bolts of cloth, over 7,000 rounds of rifle ammunition, three Mauser pistols, and four flintlock guns. The puppet army mutinied, and two platoon leaders, Li and Liu, defected with two light machine guns. The puppet army suffered 19 casualties, while our side suffered no casualties or losses.

Battle of Gaolingzi, Middle East Railway 108

On May 23, Li Zhenhua, commander of the 7th Detachment of our army's guerrillas, led his troops to engage the 10th Regiment of the puppet army, led by Regiment Commander Wen, with two companies, the 3rd and 4th, in the Gaolingzi area. After a two-hour standoff, the puppet army, seeing their unfavorable terrain and unwilling soldiers, retreated, saying, "Please retreat, old generals. You are the army that saves the country. Slaves of the country cannot save the country, nor can they fight those who save the country. Let our dog slave regimental commander do it alone. Old generals, there's no need to risk your lives. Company commanders, let's go!" and throwing down their guns to flee. Captain Li gathered the team and searched the battlefield, obtaining many abandoned guns and ammunition before returning to the team. In this battle, the puppet army lost one platoon leader and two wounded soldiers. Our side had 12 wounded soldiers and no other losses.

Construction Bank Decides to Invest RMB 5.5 Million in the Construction of the Cao'e River Railway Bridge on the Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway to Complete the Entire Line 115

Shenshi News Agency reports: The China Construction Bank was established on the 4th of this month and is actively carrying out business operations. A Shenshi News Agency reporter learned from banking circles yesterday that the company's first business has been determined to be an investment of RMB 5.5 million in the construction of the Cao'e River Railway Bridge on the Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway. The details are as follows:

Completing the Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway: The Construction Bank was originally intended to support construction work and bears a heavy responsibility. It is extremely cautious in terms of investment. The previous rumor that it would invest in the Central Machinery Factory is still under discussion. According to reliable sources in the banking world that the reporter obtained yesterday, the first business after the opening of the Construction Bank has been determined to be an investment in the construction of the Cao'e River Railway Bridge on the Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway. The amount of investment has been agreed to be RMB 5.5 million, with a portion of the operating income of the railway as collateral. The Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway currently only runs to Hangzhou and from Baiguan to Ningbo. The section in between, from Hangzhou through Xiaoshan and Shaoxing to Baiguan, has not yet been completed. In addition to the Qiantang River Bridge, which has been separately contacted with Shanghai banking circles to borrow funds for construction, the remaining tracks that urgently need to be completed require approximately RMB 10 million. In addition to the RMB 4.5 million that the Sino-British Bank has agreed to reinvest, the remaining RMB 5.5 million will be invested by the Construction Bank.

Constructing the Cao'e River Bridge: At the same time, it is also stipulated that a portion of the funds will be used for the construction of the Cao'e River Bridge. Before the European War, a German company contracted to build the Cao'e River Railway Bridge and had completed part of the base-filling work. Later, due to the outbreak of the war, it was suspended. Reconstructing it this time can save a portion of the project. When the two major bridges, the Cao'e River Bridge and the Qiantang River Bridge, are completed, the Shanghai-Hangzhou Railway and the Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway will be fully connected.

Expanding the Board of Directors and Supervisors: The China Construction Bank has expanded its leased office in the Continental Building on Jiujiang Road to six large rooms to cope with the increased workload after its opening. As for expanding the board of directors by four people and the supervisors by two people, after the shareholders' meeting has resolved and passed it, they are now looking for candidates. As soon as Chairman Kong Xiangxi returns to Shanghai, it can be formally announced.

Dr. Wu Lien-teh Discusses the Meeting of the League of Nations Health Committee: Dr. Rajchman Will Not Come to China This Year, the League of Nations Congratulates China on Its Achievements 116

The North China Daily News reports: After Dr. Wu Lien-teh arrived in Shanghai yesterday (the 7th), a representative of the North China Daily News visited him and asked whether Dr. Rajchman would return to China. Dr. Wu could not give a definite answer, but said that Dr. Rajchman would not come to China again this year. Dr. Rajchman's term as Director of the League of Nations Technical Expert Group in China was for one year. Although the term has expired, his position as Health Advisor to the Chinese Ministry of Health will not expire until August of this year. Whether he will be re-appointed will be decided at that time. Dr. Wu then described the meeting of the Geneva Health Committee, saying that the meeting had discussed Chinese affairs for a whole morning. He had submitted a report on the progress of health work in China since 1931, which was divided into four parts: (1) demonstrating the progress of central health undertakings and the Central Hospital in the capital; (2) China's epidemic prevention affairs, focusing on four central points; (3) the situation of cholera in China; (4) the progress of national isolation affairs in the past three years. The four central points of epidemic prevention are Outer Baikal, Tongliao, Shanxi, and Fujian. After 20 years of work, the plague in Outer Baikal has been completely eliminated. Tongliao is now in the hands of the Japanese and cannot be described. After he reported the epidemic prevention situation in Shanxi to the League of Nations Committee, the League of Nations Committee decided to cooperate with China and set up a research center in a certain county in the province. As for Fujian Province, it is heard that there have been outbreaks of plague again this summer. Dr. Wu continued to point out the great progress in controlling cholera epidemics, especially in Shanghai. Few people have died from it recently, mostly due to the people receiving vaccinations and the timely opening of seasonal epidemic hospitals every year. After he submitted the report to the League of Nations Committee, he further informed them that the ninth triennial conference of the Far Eastern Tropical Medical Association was scheduled to be held in Nanjing from October 1st to 10th of this year. All countries in the Far East have been invited to send representatives to China to attend the meeting. The League of Nations Executive Committee has also received this request and has decided to send three medical doctors, Parker, Posyk, and Strangpo, as representatives. Dr. Wu concluded by saying that the League of Nations representatives all congratulated China on the many undertakings completed in a short period of three years. Dr. Rajchman also attended the meeting several times and expressed his observations on overseas health work, especially praising the development of sports in China. Two days later, he submitted a complete report on the League of Nations' technical cooperation with China to the League of Nations Executive Council, which was fully accepted.

Provincial and Municipal Governments Must Not Increase Various Export Taxes 117

The Executive Yuan, based on a proposal by the Ministry of Finance to reduce and exempt various export taxes to promote the development of domestic industries and expand overseas trade channels, issued an instruction to provincial and municipal governments yesterday that no additional taxes or levies should be added in the future. The original order is as follows: It is hereby noted that, according to a proposal previously submitted by the Ministry of Finance to reduce and exempt various export taxes and revise tax rates, the matter was resolved and passed at the 161st meeting of this Yuan, submitted to the 409th meeting of the Central Political Conference, resolved in principle and passed, and submitted to the Legislative Yuan for deliberation and amendment before being promulgated by the National Government by decree. A clear order has already been issued to all parties to inform them of the matter. It is noted that in recent years, our country's major export commodities have mostly shown a state of stagnation. The reason for this is, of course, the impact of the global economic panic, but high freight rates and heavy taxes and levies are all sufficient to strike a blow to export goods. The Ministry of Finance's proposal to change the tax rates this time is to promote the development of domestic industries, expand overseas trade channels, and reduce the burden on merchants. Since the promulgation of the revised tax rates, the provincial and municipal governments concerned must not increase any additional taxes or levies on the various goods exempt from export tax in the revised plan in the future, in order to conform to the central government's intention to promote industry and show consideration for the difficulties of merchants. In addition to separate orders, it is hereby ordered that they be followed and that all subordinates be instructed to follow suit. This order.

Inland Parcel Tax to Be Levied Uniformly Starting Tomorrow to Prevent Merchants from Taking Advantage and Evading Taxes 119

The Jianghai Customs authorities collect parcel taxes on parcels coming and going by post, assigning personnel to inspect and handle them at the General Post Office. However, inland parcels sent from one inland location to another do not go through the General Post Office, so they are not taxed. As a result, some merchants transport goods from Shanghai to inland post offices near Shanghai for shipment in order to evade taxes. Although the Customs authorities have strictly investigated and prohibited this, it is ultimately difficult to prevent. Now, the Jianghai Customs has repeatedly reported that some merchants are increasingly evading taxes, which is detrimental to commercial transportation. Commissioner of Customs Robert Brooke deeply feels that if this continues without rectification, it will have a profound impact on tax revenue. Therefore, he has submitted a request to the Ministry of Finance to levy taxes on inland parcels uniformly starting tomorrow.

Two Railways Revise Freight Rates for Bulky and Explosive Goods 121

The traffic departments of the Beijing-Shanghai and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railways issued a notice yesterday to all transfer companies and stationmasters, stating, "For the purpose of notification, the loading and unloading fee rates for bulky and explosive goods are hereby revised, to be implemented from July 10. The loading and unloading fee rates for explosive hazards and bulky goods stipulated in the notice of December 22, 1933, shall be cancelled at the same time. The newly revised price rates are copied and issued herewith for your compliance." The new revised handling rates for bulky explosives are as follows: (1) Bulky goods: Any goods whose weight exceeds 350 kilograms per piece are considered bulky goods. Whether transported by the whole car or less-than-carload, the price is calculated by adding to the normal loading and unloading fee rates. If bulky goods are loaded together with non-bulky goods, the fees must be calculated separately, that is, the bulky pieces are charged according to the bulky goods rate, and the non-bulky pieces are charged according to the non-bulky rate. When calculating the tonnage, the tonnage of the bulky pieces should be converted first (that is, if it is less than one metric ton, it is also calculated as one metric ton), and the tonnage of the bulky pieces should be subtracted from the total car tonnage, and the remainder is the tonnage of the non-bulky pieces (for example, if 30 tons of goods are shipped from the Shanghai North Station in one whole car, and one piece weighs 650 kilograms, then one ton of bulky goods should be charged 40 cents, which is twice the normal rate of 20 cents per metric ton, and 29 tons should be charged 5 yuan and 80 cents for bulky goods loading fees, which is 20 cents per metric ton, 29 tons is 5 yuan and 80 cents. If there are two pieces of 800 kilograms and one piece of 355 kilograms, then two tons of bulky goods should be charged 80 cents for loading fees and 28 tons of non-bulky goods should be charged 5 yuan and 60 cents for loading fees, and so on). (2) Explosives: Those stipulated in pages 127 to 129 of the Freight Classification Table shall be calculated at twice the prescribed ordinary loading and unloading fee rate, regardless of the weight of each piece (for example, if 250 kilograms are shipped from the North Station, one piece, then the loading fee should be 20 cents, two cents for every 50 kilograms, doubled to four cents). (Note) Loading and unloading fees should be calculated according to the weight of the railway freight, but explosives should be charged freight at a minimum of two tons in accordance with the regulations. Now that it has been stipulated that the loading and unloading fee for explosives should be doubled, the rule of charging loading fees at a minimum of two tons no longer applies. (3) If loading and unloading is done with a crane and assisted by workers, it should be calculated according to the prescribed ordinary loading and unloading fee rate.

Record of the Meeting of the South Shanghai Rent Reduction Association 127

The South Shanghai Rent Reduction Association held a joint meeting of the executive committee of its branch associations yesterday at the Association's hall in Yongqing Lane, Minquan Road. Those present included Shao Tinglu, Lin Houfang, Wu Zaitang, Gu Xiayun, Wang Wanzhang, Yang Qiqing, Wu B善, etc. Shen Xinfu presided over the meeting, and Ni Yiguan served as the recorder. The following resolutions were passed: (1) Regarding the cases of landlords Zhang Dingxin Soy Sauce Garden and Lei Yushang Pharmacy on Minquan Road, and landlord Shen Xingchu of Sanpin Lane, Da Lin Road, who were requested by the Association to reduce rents to maintain market conditions, and who have successively replied, tentatively agreeing to a 10% reduction, and sending representatives to the Association for consultation on how to handle the matter, it was resolved that the opinions of the tenants should be solicited before further review. (2) The Association's special publication has been published once a week. In addition to mailing over 2,000 copies to various institutions, organizations, schools, and prominent figures in Beijing and Shanghai, how should the remaining copies be distributed to businesses and residents, given the high cost? It was resolved that members should be assigned to distribute them widely. Those willing to assist wholeheartedly should pay a small fee of 2 jiao for printing paper each month and must be given a receipt with the Association's seal. No extra demands are allowed. Because the publication progresses systematically and contains rent reduction information based on reason and legality, both landlords and tenants who are concerned about the market situation and paying attention to rent reduction should have a copy for reference. (3) The rent reduction movement has become unstoppable, and it is inevitable that it will last for a long time, leading to transgressive actions. How should this be prevented? It was resolved that for any request for rent reduction, whether in the name of a branch association or an individual, the Association should submit a written request to the landlord. Before the consultation is resolved, the rent should be deposited in the bank. If the landlord comes to collect the rent, the deposit book must be presented for inspection. However, the Association will not be involved in any rent reduction actions that have not been registered with the Association, whether by a group or individual. Even if a branch association or individual has registered with the Association, if they do not act in accordance with the Association's regulations, they will not be protected. (4) The Association has repeatedly received letters from landlords who find it difficult to comply with rent reduction in practice, generally stating that rents are already difficult to collect due to rent reduction, and they are already low but are being asked to be lowered further. Those who do not rely on rent for their livelihood can console themselves with righteousness, but for those who lack the ability to work or are widowed and rely on this small amount of rent to maintain their livelihoods, it is tantamount to destroying their lives. The wording is sincere. How should this be handled? It was resolved that tenants should not demand rent reductions if the rent has not been increased for more than six years, or if the landlord lacks the ability to work or is widowed and relies on a small amount of property to maintain their livelihood. If the landlord meets the above conditions, the Association will do its best to protect them. (5) The representative of Chengzhi Lane reported that the representative verbally agreed to a reduction of several yuan per month. How should this be resolved in terms of percentage? It was resolved that it should be reviewed after consultation between both parties. (6) The representative of Zhao Fang Lane reported that the landlord had already agreed to a 10% reduction, but the tenant still felt it was too high, leading the landlord to file a lawsuit. The judge instructed both parties not to be stubborn and to go out for reconciliation, but it has not been established yet. How should this be handled? It was resolved to send a letter to the landlord to resolve it with a 15% reduction. The meeting adjourned after the discussions.

The License Tax is Transferred to the Municipal Finance Bureau. The Cigarette Exchange Association Held a Meeting Yesterday 129

It has been found that cigarette and alcohol licenses have been paid in two installments over the years. Since 1928, cigarette licenses have been changed to four seasons. Shanghai's Chinese and foreign concessions are adjacent to each other, and the situation is special. Cigarette merchants cannot bear any further burden. A letter was sent to the authorities requesting a flexible solution. The authorities were sympathetic to the difficulties of the merchants, and the payment of the license tax was changed to quarterly, and the amount was changed to half. So far, they have been at peace with each other. The license tax is now ordered by the Ministry of Finance to be transferred to the Shanghai Municipal Government Finance Bureau for continuation. The industry has not understood the truth and has become panicked. Therefore, yesterday (the 8th) at 3 pm, a joint meeting of the executive supervisors was convened and resolved to explain the historical evolution over the years and send a letter to the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce to request the Municipal Government Finance Bureau to allow the continuation of the usual practice in order to relieve the difficulties of the merchants and ensure the peace of business.

The Invoices of Soda Bottles Are Coming Off, The Inspectors Thought It was Tax Evasion and Detained Them. 130

Yongfaxiang requests the Industry Association to negotiate and return them.

Yongfaxiang Cigarette Exchange Shop at No. 61 Dalin Road, Xiaoximen, had its soda bottles detained by the Invoice Tax Bureau inspectors because the invoice was coming off due to water. They requested the Cigarette Exchange Industry Association to negotiate for their return. The original letter is recorded below: Dear Sirs, Our shop sells soda and purchases invoices in accordance with the regulations, and affixes them to the bottles for sale. On the 2nd of this month, an inspector from the Shanghai Invoice Tax Bureau came to the store to inspect the soda. The invoices were affixed in full without omission, which was fortunately certified by the police officers of the Second District. However, among the hundreds of empty bottles in stock returned by customers, 112 bottles had fallen off their invoices due to freezing and moisture after opening. The inspector mistakenly thought that it was tax evasion and detained them all, sending them to the bureau to wait for a penalty, etc. The water sold by the factory is purchased by the soda business that originally shipped the goods, who first purchases enough invoices and issues invoices, and then holds the freight receipt of the tax bureau for inspection along the way. Once it arrives at the store, it is immediately entered into the goods source register, then the invoices are affixed to the bottles, and then they are sold. We have asked ourselves and found no errors. Now, we are being detained innocently and forced to be punished, which is really inappropriate. Therefore, we are sending a letter to your association to uphold justice and quickly send someone to investigate in order to clarify the truth. We should ask the authorities to deal with it fairly and return the detained empty bottles in full in order to maintain commercial transport and ensure the peace of business, etc.

The National Products Association Telegraphed the Ministry of Finance, Asking it to Correct the Extortion of the Shangbao Tax Bureau, Regarding the Undeserved Deduction of Fines for Yili Soda 131

The Shanghai Citizens' Association for the Promotion of National Products, regarding the Shangbao Invoice Tax Bureau's harsh treatment of the Yili Soda Company's empty bottle fine, resolved at the eighth joint meeting of the fourteenth session of the executive supervisors yesterday to telegraph the Ministry of Finance and immediately order a correction. The original telegram read: Minister Kong Jun of the Ministry of Finance, according to a letter from member Yili Soda Company of the affiliated association, the member specially sailed the Yili ship on June 30 to welcome and send leaders from all walks of life to Putuo for summer vacation, without taking boat fares, providing meals, and supplying soda. At that time, 20 boxes of this brand of soda were loaded, originally intended to be given to tourists to relieve the heat, and invoices were affixed in accordance with the regulations, and they had been inspected and stamped by the Shangbao Invoice Tax Bureau. Unexpectedly, when the ship returned to Shanghai yesterday morning, the inspector of the bureau falsely accused the 20 boxes of empty bottles loaded on the ship of not having invoices affixed and ordered a fine of 20 yuan. They had no choice but to pay the full amount to the bureau and receive a receipt under duress. Recently, we have heard that the government has abolished exorbitant taxes and miscellaneous fees, and has issued three orders and five applications to relieve the difficulties of merchants. Moreover, the taxation of national products is only once and can be circulated. However, the director of the bureau dared to despise the laws and regulations, extort the people, and act tyrannically and illegally. Therefore, a special letter is sent to request your association to relieve the suffering of the national products industry and ask for relief in order to eliminate corruption, etc. It has been found that the member entertained people from all walks of life to travel to Putuo and gave them soda to drink, and taxes have been paid in accordance with the regulations. However, a fine was imposed for transporting back empty bottles, which not only violates the government's good intentions to exempt exorbitant taxes and miscellaneous fees but also violates the national product's one-item, one-tax system. Invoice harassment has reached its extreme, and the false accusations and harsh fines are extremely painful. In addition to sending a letter to the bureau to exempt the fine, a special telegram is sent to request your Excellency to immediately order a correction in order to maintain national products and relieve the difficulties of merchants, which would be a great virtue. Yu Hede and others, Standing Committee Members of the Fourteenth Session of the Shanghai Citizens' Association for the Promotion of National Products, respectfully bow and affix their seals.
